### [74] [ConsistencyAI: A Benchmark to Assess LLMs' Factual Consistency When Responding to Different Demographic Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13852)
*Peter Banyas,Shristi Sharma,Alistair Simmons,Atharva Vispute*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究引入了 ConsistencyAI，一个独立的基准，用于衡量大型语言模型（LLMs）在不同个体身份下的事实一致性。研究发现，不同身份的提问可能导致 LLM 给出事实不一致的回答，并且这种不一致性因模型和主题而异。研究发布了代码和演示以促进可复现的评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LLMs）在信息传播中的作用日益增强，确保它们提供的事实信息在不同用户群体中保持一致至关重要。然而，目前缺乏一个独立且全面的基准来衡量 LLMs 在面对不同个体身份（如不同的年龄、性别、地域等）时，回答事实信息时的一致性。LLMs 可能会因为用户的身份而调整其回答，这可能导致事实上的不一致，从而影响信息的可靠性和用户的信任度。因此，有必要开发一个独立于 LLM 提供商的基准，以评估和提高 LLMs 的事实一致性。

Method: 该研究引入了一个名为 ConsistencyAI 的独立基准，用于衡量 LLMs 在不同个体身份下的事实一致性。研究团队使用了 19 个 LLMs，针对 15 个主题，每个主题要求模型提供 5 个事实。为了模拟不同用户身份，研究人员为每次查询添加了来自不同个体身份的提示语境，并重复了 100 次。为了量化事实一致性，研究人员将模型的回应转换为句嵌入，计算了不同身份回应之间的余弦相似度，并计算了加权平均余弦相似度作为事实一致性得分。该研究还确定了一个基准阈值（0.8656），并对不同模型和主题的表现进行了排名和比较。

Result: 在 100 个个体身份的实验中，LLMs 的事实一致性得分范围从 0.9065 到 0.7896，平均得分为 0.8656，该平均分被确定为基准阈值。研究发现，xAI 的 Grok-3 模型表现出最高的一致性，而一些轻量级模型则得分最低。事实一致性也因主题而异：关于就业市场的主题一致性最低，而关于 G7 国家领导人的信息最一致。对于疫苗接种或以色列-巴勒斯坦冲突等敏感话题，不同提供商的 LLMs 表现出显著的分歧。这些结果表明，模型的提供商和信息的具体主题都会影响事实的一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了 LLMs 在不同个体身份下可能存在事实不一致性的问题，并提出了 ConsistencyAI 作为衡量这一问题的独立基准。研究结果表明，LLMs 的事实一致性受到模型提供商和信息主题的双重影响，并且存在显著差异。为了提高 LLMs 的可靠性和可信度，研究人员呼吁开发和采用“个体身份无关”的提示策略。此外，他们还发布了代码和交互式演示，以支持可复现的评估，并鼓励社区进一步研究和改进 LLMs 的事实一致性。未来的工作可以扩展测试的主题范围，探索更多样的个体身份，并研究导致不一致性的具体原因。

Abstract: Is an LLM telling you different facts than it's telling me? This paper
introduces ConsistencyAI, an independent benchmark for measuring the factual
consistency of large language models (LLMs) for different personas.
ConsistencyAI tests whether, when users of different demographics ask identical
questions, the model responds with factually inconsistent answers. Designed
without involvement from LLM providers, this benchmark offers impartial
evaluation and accountability. In our experiment, we queried 19 LLMs with
prompts that requested 5 facts for each of 15 topics. We repeated this query
100 times for each LLM, each time adding prompt context from a different
persona selected from a subset of personas modeling the general population. We
processed the responses into sentence embeddings, computed cross-persona cosine
similarity, and computed the weighted average of cross-persona cosine
similarity to calculate factual consistency scores. In 100-persona experiments,
scores ranged from 0.9065 to 0.7896, and the mean was 0.8656, which we adopt as
a benchmark threshold. xAI's Grok-3 is most consistent, while several
lightweight models rank lowest. Consistency varies by topic: the job market is
least consistent, G7 world leaders most consistent, and issues like vaccines or
the Israeli-Palestinian conflict diverge by provider. These results show that
both the provider and the topic shape the factual consistency. We release our
code and interactive demo to support reproducible evaluation and encourage
persona-invariant prompting strategies.

</details>


### [75] [InsurTech innovation using natural language processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21112)
*Panyi Dong,Zhiyu Quan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统保险公司面临InsurTech的竞争，需要利用替代数据源和先进技术（如NLP）来处理非结构化文本数据，以改进现有保险业务，尤其是在商业保险定价和风险评估方面，从而保持竞争力。

Method: 本文结合了概念性概述和实际案例研究。研究人员利用InsurTech合作伙伴提供的真实世界替代数据，结合传统保险数据，应用了多种NLP技术，包括特征去偏、特征压缩和行业分类，以处理非结构化文本数据。

Result: 研究结果表明，NLP技术能够从非结构化文本中提取有价值的特征，这些特征能够丰富和优化商业保险的定价因素，并引入新的行业分类技术来评估潜在风险。NLP处理后的数据为决策提供了新的视角。

Conclusion: NLP不仅仅是一个辅助工具，而是现代数据驱动的保险分析的基石。通过NLP技术，保险公司能够更有效地利用数据，优化定价，改进风险评估，并在日益激烈的市场竞争中保持优势。

Abstract: With the rapid rise of InsurTech, traditional insurance companies are
increasingly exploring alternative data sources and advanced technologies to
sustain their competitive edge. This paper provides both a conceptual overview
and practical case studies of natural language processing (NLP) and its
emerging applications within insurance operations, focusing on transforming
raw, unstructured text into structured data suitable for actuarial analysis and
decision-making. Leveraging real-world alternative data provided by an
InsurTech industry partner that enriches traditional insurance data sources, we
apply various NLP techniques to demonstrate feature de-biasing, feature
compression, and industry classification in the commercial insurance context.
These enriched, text-derived insights not only add to and refine traditional
rating factors for commercial insurance pricing but also offer novel
perspectives for assessing underlying risk by introducing novel industry
classification techniques. Through these demonstrations, we show that NLP is
not merely a supplementary tool but a foundational element of modern,
data-driven insurance analytics.

### [76] [MAD-Fact: A Multi-Agent Debate Framework for Long-Form Factuality Evaluation in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22967)
*Yucheng Ning,Xixun Lin,Fang Fang,Yanan Cao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个名为LongHalluQA的新型中文长文本事实性数据集，并开发了一个名为MAD-Fact的多主体验证系统，以解决大型语言模型（LLMs）在长文本生成中事实准确性不足的问题。研究结果表明，更大的模型在事实一致性上表现更好，而国内模型在中文内容上具有优势。该框架旨在提升LLMs在生物医学、法律和教育等高风险领域的安全应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLMs）在事实准确性方面存在普遍担忧，尤其是在生物医学、法律和教育等高风险领域。针对短文本的现有评估方法在处理长文本时效果不佳，因为长文本涉及复杂的推理链、交织的观点和累积的信息。因此，需要一种系统性的方法来评估和提高LLMs长文本输出的事实可靠性。

Method: 研究人员构建了一个名为LongHalluQA的中文长文本事实性数据集，并开发了一个基于辩论的多主体验证系统MAD-Fact。他们还引入了一个事实重要性层次结构，以捕捉长文本中不同声明的重要程度。通过在两个基准测试上进行实验来评估该方法。

Result: 实验结果显示，更大的LLMs模型在事实一致性方面通常表现更好。国内模型在处理中文内容时表现尤为出色。该研究提供了一个结构化的框架，用于评估和增强LLMs长文本输出的事实可靠性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了长文本事实性评估所需的数据集和验证系统，为LLMs在敏感领域的安全部署提供了指导。研究结果强调了模型规模和语言特异性对事实准确性的影响。未来的工作可以进一步扩展数据集，优化多主体验证机制，并探索更复杂的长文本评估指标。

Abstract: The widespread adoption of Large Language Models (LLMs) raises critical
concerns about the factual accuracy of their outputs, especially in high-risk
domains such as biomedicine, law, and education. Existing evaluation methods
for short texts often fail on long-form content due to complex reasoning
chains, intertwined perspectives, and cumulative information. To address this,
we propose a systematic approach integrating large-scale long-form datasets,
multi-agent verification mechanisms, and weighted evaluation metrics. We
construct LongHalluQA, a Chinese long-form factuality dataset; and develop
MAD-Fact, a debate-based multi-agent verification system. We introduce a fact
importance hierarchy to capture the varying significance of claims in long-form
texts. Experiments on two benchmarks show that larger LLMs generally maintain
higher factual consistency, while domestic models excel on Chinese content. Our
work provides a structured framework for evaluating and enhancing factual
reliability in long-form LLM outputs, guiding their safe deployment in
sensitive domains.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种零样本实体链接器，利用大型语言模型（LLM）。该方法的核心创新在于，通过在LLM的倒数第二层评估“yes”令牌的对数概率来重新排序候选实体。这种方法避免了对特定数据集的显式训练，实现了零样本学习。

Result: 文章展示了所提出的零样本实体链接器在DBLP 2025知识图谱上的性能。虽然具体的量化指标未在摘要中提供，但其零样本能力和基于LLM的方法被认为是关键的成果，表明了该方法在处理新数据和新实体类型方面的潜力。

Conclusion: 本文成功地开发了一种新颖的零样本实体链接方法，利用LLM和基于对数概率的重排序策略，为DBLP知识图谱的最新版本提供了有效的实体链接解决方案。该方法在不依赖显式训练数据的情况下，展现了处理新实体类型和版本的能力，为未来的实体链接研究提供了新的方向。

Abstract: In this work we present an entity linker for DBLP's 2025 version of RDF-based
Knowledge Graph. Compared to the 2022 version, DBLP now considers publication
venues as a new entity type called dblp:Stream. In the earlier version of
DBLPLink, we trained KG-embeddings and re-rankers on a dataset to produce
entity linkings. In contrast, in this work, we develop a zero-shot entity
linker using LLMs using a novel method, where we re-rank candidate entities
based on the log-probabilities of the "yes" token output at the penultimate
layer of the LLM.

### [78] [SimulMEGA: MoE Routers are Advanced Policy Makers for Simultaneous Speech Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01200)
*Chenyang Le,Bing Han,Jinshun Li,Songyong Chen,Yanmin Qian*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SimulMEGA是一个无监督策略学习框架，通过结合前缀式训练和混合专家精炼器，隐式地学习有效的读写决策，以应对SimulST中的翻译质量、延迟和语义连贯性之间的挑战，尤其是在多语言多对多场景下。该方法在六种语言对上进行了评估，其语音转文本模型在延迟1.5秒时BLEU下降不到7%，在延迟3秒时下降不到3%，优于Seamless基线，并成功扩展到流式TTS任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的同步语音翻译（SimulST）系统在严格的延迟限制下，难以平衡翻译质量、延迟和语义连贯性，特别是在多语言多对多的场景中，读写策略不一致阻碍了统一策略的学习。

Method: SimulMEGA（Simultaneous Generation by Mixture-of-Experts Gating）框架采用无监督策略学习，结合前缀式训练和混合专家精炼器，隐式学习读写策略，无推理时间开销。该设计仅需对标准Transformer架构进行最小修改，并可推广到语音到文本和文本到语音的流式任务。

Result: 在六种语言对上的全面评估显示，SimulMEGA的5亿参数语音转文本模型优于Seamless基线，在1.5秒平均延迟下BLEU下降不到7%，在3秒延迟下下降不到3%。将其扩展到单向骨干的流式TTS任务也取得了优越的延迟-质量权衡。

Conclusion: SimulMEGA提供了一种有效的无监督学习框架，用于解决SimulST中的挑战，并在语音转文本和流式TTS任务中展现出优越的性能和通用性。

Abstract: Simultaneous Speech Translation (SimulST) enables real-time cross-lingual
communication by jointly optimizing speech recognition and machine translation
under strict latency constraints. Existing systems struggle to balance
translation quality, latency, and semantic coherence, particularly in
multilingual many-to-many scenarios where divergent read and write policies
hinder unified strategy learning. In this paper, we present SimulMEGA
(Simultaneous Generation by Mixture-of-Experts Gating), an unsupervised policy
learning framework that combines prefix-based training with a
Mixture-of-Experts refiner to learn effective read and write decisions in an
implicit manner, without adding inference-time overhead. Our design requires
only minimal modifications to standard transformer architectures and
generalizes across both speech-to-text and text-to-speech streaming tasks.
Through comprehensive evaluation on six language pairs, our 500M parameter
speech-to-text model outperforms the Seamless baseline, achieving under 7
percent BLEU degradation at 1.5 seconds average lag and under 3 percent at 3
seconds. We further demonstrate the versatility of SimulMEGA by extending it to
streaming TTS with a unidirectional backbone, yielding superior latency quality
tradeoffs.

Conclusion: WEST (WE Speech Toolkit) 是一个创新的、基于 LLM 的语音工具包，它通过提供全栈能力、易用性和可扩展性，解决了现有语音工具包的局限性。 WEST 为语音技术的研究和应用提供了一个强大的平台，有望推动语音交互和理解的进一步发展。未来的工作可以集中在进一步扩展其多模态能力和优化模型以适应更多特定场景。

Abstract: In this paper, we present WEST(WE Speech Toolkit), a speech toolkit based on
a large language model (LLM) for speech understanding, generation, and
interaction. There are three key features of WEST: 1) Fully LLM-based: Standing
on the shoulders of giants by reusing mature architectures, ecosystems (e.g.,
Hugging Face), and methods (e.g., sequence packing) from large models. 2)
Full-stack: Supports tasks such as recognition, synthesis, understanding,
dialogue, and multimodal capabilities, with extensibility to incorporate
open-source models. 3) Simple and Stupid: A simple and stupid speech toolkit
that everyone can Touch. In addition, WEST provides two types of recipes,
models, and experimental results. The first is entirely based on open-source
models and open-source data, allowing users to fully reproduce the experiments
in this paper and serving as a verification system or minimal system baseline.
The second is trained on massive data, offering superior performance so the
user can directly apply it out of the box. WEST is publicly avilable at
https://github.com/wenet-e2e/west/

### [80] [SciReasoner: Laying the Scientific Reasoning Ground Across Disciplines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.21320)
*Yizhou Wang,Chen Tang,Han Deng,Jiabei Xiao,Jiaqi Liu,Jianyu Wu,Jun Yao,Pengze Li,Encheng Su,Lintao Wang,Guohang Zhuang,Yuchen Ren,Ben Fei,Ming Hu,Xin Chen,Dongzhan Zhou,Junjun He,Xiangyu Yue,Zhenfei Yin,Jiamin Wu,Qihao Zheng,Yuhao Zhou,Huihui Xu,Chenglong Ma,Yan Lu,Wenlong Zhang,Chunfeng Song,Philip Torr,Shixiang Tang,Xinzhu Ma,Wanli Ouyang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个名为 SciReason 的科学推理基础模型，能够将自然语言与异构科学表征对齐。模型在包含科学文本、纯序列和序列-文本对的 206B 标记语料库上进行预训练，然后通过 40M 指令的 SFT、冷启动引导以引出长篇思维链，以及带有任务特定奖励塑造的强化学习进行对齐，从而培养了严谨的科学推理能力。该模型支持四种能力家族，涵盖工作流中的多达 103 项任务，包括文本与科学格式之间的忠实翻译、文本/知识提取、属性预测、属性分类，以及无条件和有条件序列生成与设计。与现有专家系统相比，该模型拓宽了指令覆盖范围，改善了跨领域泛化能力，并提高了保真度。研究中详细介绍了数据整理和训练过程，并证明了跨学科学习能够增强迁移和下游可靠性。最后，研究将模型、指令调优数据集和评估代码开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言与异构科学表征（如图表、方程式等）之间的鸿沟阻碍了科学知识的整合与利用。现有的模型通常专注于特定领域或特定任务，缺乏通用性、跨领域泛化能力和严谨的科学推理能力。本研究旨在弥合这一差距，开发一个能够理解和生成多种科学表征，并进行复杂科学推理的基础模型，以促进科学发现和知识传播。

Method: 1. **预训练：** 在包含科学文本、纯序列（如基因组数据）和序列-文本对（如蛋白质序列及其描述）的 206B 标记的大规模语料库上进行预训练，以建立对科学数据的广泛理解。
2. **指令微调 (SFT)：** 使用 4000 万条指令对模型进行微调，以使其能够遵循人类指令并执行特定任务。
3. **冷启动引导 (Annealed Cold-Start Bootstrapping)：** 采用一种特殊的引导技术，旨在激发模型生成长篇、连贯的“思维链”推理过程，模仿人类解决复杂问题的步骤。
4. **强化学习 (RL)：** 结合任务特定的奖励塑造，对模型进行强化学习训练，以优化其在科学推理任务上的表现，使其能够进行更深思熟虑的推理。
5. **能力设计：** 模型被设计支持四种核心能力家族，涵盖了从数据转换到预测和生成的广泛任务。
6. **数据与评估：** 详细说明了数据整理和训练过程，并提供了开源的模型、数据集和评估代码以供社区使用。

Result: 与现有的专业系统相比，SciReason 模型在以下方面表现出优势：
1. **拓宽指令覆盖范围：** 能够处理比专业系统更广泛的指令类型。
2. **改善跨领域泛化：** 在不同科学领域之间具有更好的泛化能力。
3. **增强保真度：** 在执行任务时能够保持更高的准确性和忠实度。
此外，研究表明跨学科学习（即在包含多种学科数据的语料库上训练）能够显著增强模型的迁移学习能力和下游任务的可靠性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发并开源了一个名为 SciReason 的科学推理基础模型，它能够有效地对齐自然语言和异构科学表征，并进行严谨的科学推理。该模型通过大规模预训练、指令微调、冷启动引导和强化学习等先进技术实现，在多项科学任务上展现出优于现有专家系统的性能，尤其在指令覆盖、跨领域泛化和保真度方面。研究强调了跨学科学习的重要性，它能提升模型的迁移能力和可靠性。SciReason 的开源将极大地推动科学研究和应用的发展，但未来仍需探索其在处理更复杂、更长推理链以及在更多新兴科学领域的应用潜力。

Abstract: We present a scientific reasoning foundation model that aligns natural
language with heterogeneous scientific representations. The model is pretrained
on a 206B-token corpus spanning scientific text, pure sequences, and
sequence-text pairs, then aligned via SFT on 40M instructions, annealed
cold-start bootstrapping to elicit long-form chain-of-thought, and
reinforcement learning with task-specific reward shaping, which instills
deliberate scientific reasoning. It supports four capability families, covering
up to 103 tasks across workflows: (i) faithful translation between text and
scientific formats, (ii) text/knowledge extraction, (iii) property prediction,
(iv) property classification, (v) unconditional and conditional sequence
generation and design. Compared with specialist systems, our approach broadens
instruction coverage, improves cross-domain generalization, and enhances
fidelity. We detail data curation and training and show that cross-discipline
learning strengthens transfer and downstream reliability. The model, instruct
tuning datasets and the evaluation code are open-sourced at
https://huggingface.co/SciReason and
https://github.com/open-sciencelab/SciReason.

</details>


### [81] [FT-MDT: Extracting Decision Trees from Medical Texts via a Novel Low-rank Adaptation Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.04655)
*Yuheng Li,Jiechao Gao,Wei Han,Wenwen Ouyang,Wei Zhu,Hui Yi Leong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为PI-LoRA的新型低秩自适应方法，用于从临床指南和教科书中自动提取医疗决策树（MDT），解决了手动标注耗时耗力的问题。PI-LoRA通过整合梯度路径信息来优化模块间的协同作用，能够为关键模块分配更重要的秩，并修剪不重要的模块，从而提高MDT提取的效率和准确性。实验结果表明，PI-LoRA在Text2MDT任务上显著优于现有的参数高效微调方法，在保持轻量化架构的同时取得了最先进的性能，特别适用于计算资源有限的临床决策支持系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前构建临床决策支持系统所依赖的医疗决策树（MDT）的构建方法，严重依赖于耗时且费力的手动标注。这种方法不仅效率低下，而且难以扩展以适应大规模的临床数据。因此，需要一种自动化方法来从临床指南和教科书中高效、准确地提取MDT，以克服手动标注的瓶颈，并推动临床决策支持系统的发展。

Method: 研究提出了一种名为PI-LoRA（Path-Integrated LoRA）的新型低秩自适应（LoRA）方法。该方法的核心在于整合梯度路径信息，以捕捉不同模块间的协同效应。通过这种方式，PI-LoRA能够更有效地进行秩分配，确保关键模块获得恰当的秩，同时修剪不重要的模块。这种选择性的秩分配使得模型能够更聚焦于提取MDT中的关键决策路径，从而提高提取的准确性和效率。研究在临床指南数据集上进行了广泛的实验，并将PI-LoRA与现有的参数高效微调方法进行了比较，以评估其在Text2MDT任务上的性能。

Result: 在Text2MDT任务上，PI-LoRA方法取得了显著的性能提升，在准确性方面优于现有的参数高效微调方法。同时，该方法在模型复杂度上得到了大幅度降低，实现了高效和准确的模型。研究表明，PI-LoRA在保持轻量化架构的同时，达到了最先进的结果。这使其特别适合计算资源受限的临床决策支持系统。

Conclusion: PI-LoRA作为一种新颖的低秩自适应方法，成功地实现了从临床文本中自动提取医疗决策树（MDT），有效解决了手动标注的痛点。通过整合梯度路径信息，该方法能够优化秩分配，提高模型效率和准确性。实验证明，PI-LoRA在Text2MDT任务上达到了最先进的性能，并且模型轻量化，非常适用于资源受限的临床环境。未来的工作可以探索将PI-LoRA应用于更广泛的临床文本数据，并进一步优化其在复杂MDT结构提取方面的能力。

Abstract: Knowledge of the medical decision process, which can be modeled as medical
decision trees (MDTs), is critical to building clinical decision support
systems. However, current MDT construction methods rely heavily on
time-consuming and laborious manual annotation. To address this challenge, we
propose PI-LoRA (Path-Integrated LoRA), a novel low-rank adaptation method for
automatically extracting MDTs from clinical guidelines and textbooks. We
integrate gradient path information to capture synergistic effects between
different modules, enabling more effective and reliable rank allocation. This
framework ensures that the most critical modules receive appropriate rank
allocations while less important ones are pruned, resulting in a more efficient
and accurate model for extracting medical decision trees from clinical texts.
Extensive experiments on medical guideline datasets demonstrate that our
PI-LoRA method significantly outperforms existing parameter-efficient
fine-tuning approaches for the Text2MDT task, achieving better accuracy with
substantially reduced model complexity. The proposed method achieves
state-of-the-art results while maintaining a lightweight architecture, making
it particularly suitable for clinical decision support systems where
computational resources may be limited.

### [82] [Augmenting Dialog with Think-Aloud Utterances for Modeling Individual Personality Traits by LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.09158)
*Seiya Ishikura,Hiroaki Yamada,Tatsuya Hiraoka,Hiroaki Yamada,Takenobu Tokunaga*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种在对话数据中加入“出声思考”（TAU）来增强大型语言模型（LLM）对个体性格建模的方法。实验表明，使用TAU增强的数据训练的“个性化LLM”在“宜人性”和“神经质”这两个维度上比仅使用原始对话数据训练的模型更能模仿人类的性格特征。研究还发现，TAU增强的质量会影响个性化LLM的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前，在文本聊天中对个体性格进行建模仍然是一个挑战。本研究旨在通过一种新的方法来改进这一领域，即利用“出声思考”（TAU）的对话数据来训练大型语言模型（LLM），以期更好地捕捉和模仿人类的性格特征。这对于开发更具个性化和人性化的AI交互至关重要。

Method: 本研究提出了一种数据增强的方法，即在现有的对话数据中加入“出声思考”（TAU）的语句。TAU是指在说出具体的话之前，将说话者内心的思考过程口头表达出来。然后，使用这种TAU增强的对话数据来训练“个性化LLM”。实验通过比较使用TAU增强数据和原始对话数据训练的LLM在模仿人类“大五人格”（Big Five）特征（包括开放性、尽责性、外倾性、宜人性、神经质）方面的表现来评估模型的效果。

Result: 实验结果表明，使用TAU增强数据训练的LLM在“宜人性”（Agreeableness）和“神经质”（Neuroticism）这两个性格维度上，比使用原始对话数据训练的LLM更能准确地模仿人类的性格。此外，研究还发现，TAU增强数据的质量对个性化LLM的性能有着显著影响，高质量的TAU能够带来更好的模型表现。

Conclusion: 本研究成功地展示了通过在对话数据中加入“出声思考”（TAU）来增强LLM对个体性格建模的能力，特别是在“宜人性”和“神经质”两个维度上。这为开发更精细、更具个性化的人机交互提供了新的途径。未来的工作可以进一步探索不同类型的TAU数据以及如何更有效地利用它们来提升模型在其他性格维度上的表现，并研究TAU增强质量的具体影响机制。

Abstract: This study proposes augmenting dialog data with think-aloud utterances (TAUs)
for modeling individual personalities in text chat by LLM. TAU is a
verbalization of a speaker's thought before articulating the utterance. We
expect "persona LLMs" trained with TAU-augmented data can mimic the speaker's
personality trait better. We tested whether the trained persona LLMs obtain the
human personality with respect to Big Five, a framework characterizing human
personality traits from five aspects. The results showed that LLMs trained with
TAU-augmented data more closely align to the speakers' Agreeableness and
Neuroticism of Big Five than those trained with original dialog data. We also
found that the quality of TAU-augmentation impacts persona LLM's performance.

</details>


### [83] [A Multilingual, Large-Scale Study of the Interplay between LLM Safeguards, Personalisation, and Disinformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.12993)
*João A. Leite,Arnav Arora,Silvia Gargova,João Luz,Gustavo Sampaio,Ian Roberts,Carolina Scarton,Kalina Bontcheva*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究首次大规模、多语言地分析了大型语言模型（LLMs）生成个性化虚假信息的能力，发现即使是简单的个性化提示也能显著提高‘越狱’（绕过安全限制）的可能性，并改变语言和修辞模式以增强说服力。研究构建了一个包含160万条个性化虚假信息文本的数据集（AI-TRAITS），并揭示了当前LLMs在多语言和跨人群背景下面临的关键安全漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）能够生成类似人类的虚假信息，但其跨语言和跨人群进行个性化内容生成的能力仍未得到充分研究。本研究旨在填补这一空白，探讨LLMs在生成针对特定人群的虚假信息方面的潜力，这对于理解和应对AI驱动的虚假信息传播至关重要，具有重要的安全和社会意义。

Method: 本研究采用了‘红队测试’（red teaming）方法，针对八种最先进的大型语言模型（LLMs），使用324个虚假叙述和150个人口统计学特征（结合了国家、世代和政治取向）的组合，在英语、俄语、葡萄牙语和印地语四种语言中进行提示。这种方法旨在系统性地探测模型的安全边界和内容生成能力。实验生成了一个名为AI-TRAITS的大规模数据集，包含160万条个性化虚假信息文本。

Result: 研究结果表明，使用简单的个性化提示就能显著提高所有被测LLMs的‘越狱’（绕过安全限制）成功率，最高可达10个百分点。此外，这些提示还能改变文本的语言和修辞模式，使其更具说服力。在模型表现方面，Grok和GPT等模型在‘越狱’率和个性化得分上均超过85%。这些发现揭示了当前先进LLMs在生成个性化虚假信息方面的关键漏洞。

Conclusion: 本研究首次揭示了大型语言模型（LLMs）在生成跨语言、跨人群的个性化虚假信息方面的显著能力，并构建了一个大规模数据集（AI-TRAITS）。研究发现，个性化提示能够有效提高模型的‘越狱’率并增强虚假信息的说服力。这些结果暴露了当前LLMs在安全对齐方面存在的关键漏洞，为未来开发更有效的安全防护和多语言虚假信息检测策略奠定了基础。然而，研究也可能存在局限性，例如模型和提示的覆盖范围，未来可在此基础上扩展模型和提示的多样性，并研究更复杂的个性化策略。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate human-like disinformation, yet
their ability to personalise such content across languages and demographics
remains underexplored. This study presents the first large-scale, multilingual
analysis of persona-targeted disinformation generation by LLMs. Employing a red
teaming methodology, we prompt eight state-of-the-art LLMs with 324 false
narratives and 150 demographic personas (combinations of country, generation,
and political orientation) across four languages--English, Russian, Portuguese,
and Hindi--resulting in AI-TRAITS, a comprehensive dataset of 1.6 million
personalised disinformation texts. Results show that the use of even simple
personalisation prompts significantly increases the likelihood of jailbreaks
across all studied LLMs, up to 10 percentage points, and alters linguistic and
rhetorical patterns that enhance narrative persuasiveness. Models such as Grok
and GPT exhibited jailbreak rates and personalisation scores both exceeding
85%. These insights expose critical vulnerabilities in current state-of-the-art
LLMs and offer a foundation for improving safety alignment and detection
strategies in multilingual and cross-demographic contexts.

</details>


### [84] [Quantifying Phonosemantic Iconicity Distributionally in 6 Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14040)
*George Flint,Kaustubh Kislay*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究采用分布方法，在六种不同语言（英语、西班牙语、印地语、芬兰语、土耳其语和泰米尔语）中大规模量化语音语义 the iconicity。通过分析词缀的语音和语义相似性空间，发现了新的可解释的语音语义 the iconicity 及其跨语言模式，并对先前假设的 the iconicity 进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管语言通常被认为是任意的，但语音和语义之间存在系统性关系。本研究旨在探索这种语音语义 the iconicity 在大规模、定量层面上的表现，以及发现新的语音语义 the iconicity 现象及其跨语言模式。

Method: 本研究采用分布方法，在六种语言（英语、西班牙语、印地语、芬兰语、土耳其语和泰米尔语）中分析词缀的语音和语义相似性空间。利用一系列统计测量方法来量化语音语义 the iconicity，并识别出新的 the iconicity 现象以及跨语言模式。

Result: 研究发现了大量可解释的语音语义 the iconicity，其中许多是先前未被识别的。此外，还发现了跨语言的 the iconicity 模式。对于先前假设的五种语音语义 the iconicity，部分得到了支持，部分结果不确定。

Conclusion: 本研究通过大规模的分布分析，证明了语音语义 the iconicity 在多种语言中普遍存在，并发现了新的 the iconicity 现象和跨语言模式。研究结果为理解语言的任意性与系统性之间的关系提供了新的视角，但也指出需要进一步研究来完全阐明这些 the iconicity 的机制和范围。

Abstract: Language is, as commonly theorized, largely arbitrary. Yet, systematic
relationships between phonetics and semantics have been observed in many
specific cases. To what degree could those systematic relationships manifest
themselves in large scale, quantitative investigations--both in previously
identified and unidentified phenomena? This work undertakes a distributional
approach to quantifying phonosemantic iconicity at scale across 6 diverse
languages (English, Spanish, Hindi, Finnish, Turkish, and Tamil). In each
language, we analyze the alignment of morphemes' phonetic and semantic
similarity spaces with a suite of statistical measures, and discover an array
of interpretable phonosemantic alignments not previously identified in the
literature, along with crosslinguistic patterns. We also analyze 5 previously
hypothesized phonosemantic alignments, finding support for some such alignments
and mixed results for others.

</details>


### [85] [Are ASR foundation models generalized enough to capture features of regional dialects for low-resource languages?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23252)
*Tawsif Tashwar Dipto,Azmol Hossain,Rubayet Sabbir Faruque,Md. Rezuwan Hassan,Kanij Fatema,Tanmoy Shome,Ruwad Naswan,Md. Foriduzzaman Zihad,Mohaymen Ul Anam,Nazia Tasnim,Hasan Mahmud,Md Kamrul Hasan,Md. Mehedi Hasan Shawon,Farig Sadeque,Tahsin Reasat*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究表明，在低资源语言的标准形式上进行语音识别建模，并将方言作为微调任务，会对区域方言的自动语音识别（ASR）产生负面影响。为解决此问题，研究者开发了一个包含78小时数据的孟加拉语语音转文本（STT）语料库Ben-10，并通过语言学和数据驱动的视角进行了分析。结果发现，现有的语音基础模型在零样本和微调设置下都难以处理区域方言的ASR任务，而针对特定方言的模型训练能有效缓解这一问题。该语料库还可作为资源受限情况下的非分布（OOD）资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动语音识别（ASR）研究主要关注低资源语言的标准形式，并将方言视为一个微调任务，这种方法忽视了方言的独特性，导致在处理区域方言时效果不佳。本研究旨在探讨方言变异对ASR的影响，并提出改进方法。

Method: 研究者开发了一个包含78小时数据的孟加拉语语音转文本（STT）语料库Ben-10。他们从语言学和数据驱动的角度分析了该语料库，并评估了现有语音基础模型在零样本和微调设置下的表现。此外，他们还研究了针对特定方言进行模型训练的效果。

Result: 研究发现，现有的语音基础模型在处理区域方言ASR任务时存在显著困难，无论是在零样本还是微调设置下。所有深度学习方法在建模方言变异的语音数据时都遇到挑战。然而，通过进行特定方言的模型训练，可以有效缓解这些问题。Ben-10语料库也可作为ASR算法在资源受限情况下的非分布（OOD）资源。

Conclusion: 区域方言对方言ASR模型提出了严峻的挑战，现有的通用模型难以适应。针对特定方言进行模型训练是提高ASR性能的有效途径。Ben-10语料库的公开为未来ASR研究提供了宝贵的资源。未来的工作可以探索更有效的跨方言建模技术以及利用Ben-10语料库进行更深入的研究。

Abstract: Conventional research on speech recognition modeling relies on the canonical
form for most low-resource languages while automatic speech recognition (ASR)
for regional dialects is treated as a fine-tuning task. To investigate the
effects of dialectal variations on ASR we develop a 78-hour annotated Bengali
Speech-to-Text (STT) corpus named Ben-10. Investigation from linguistic and
data-driven perspectives shows that speech foundation models struggle heavily
in regional dialect ASR, both in zero-shot and fine-tuned settings. We observe
that all deep learning methods struggle to model speech data under dialectal
variations but dialect specific model training alleviates the issue. Our
dataset also serves as a out of-distribution (OOD) resource for ASR modeling
under constrained resources in ASR algorithms. The dataset and code developed
for this project are publicly available

</details>

### [86] [Stiff Circuit System Modeling via Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.24727)
*Weiman Yan,Yi-Chia Chang,Wanyu Zhao*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种结合Crossformer和Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks (KAN)的新方法，用于对电感电路的瞬态行为进行建模，显著提高了预测精度并降低了训练时间和错误率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的电路行为建模方法在处理像电感电路这类“硬”电路时存在挑战。精确高效的电路行为建模是现代电子设计自动化的关键，尤其是在处理这类具有挑战性的电路时，迫切需要更优的建模方法。

Method: 研究将先进的Transformer模型Crossformer（擅长时间序列预测）与Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks (KAN)相结合。Crossformer能够捕捉时间序列的特征，而KAN则增强了特征提取能力，共同用于建模电感电路的瞬态行为。实验基于模拟数字转换器（ADC）电路的SPICE仿真数据进行。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在预测电路响应方面具有更高的保真度，能够应对广泛的输入条件。与现有方法相比，该方法在训练时间和错误率方面均有显著降低。

Conclusion: 所提出的Crossformer与KAN相结合的方法，在建模电感电路瞬态行为方面表现出优越性，能够有效提高预测精度并优化训练效率。未来可进一步探索该模型在更复杂电路和更大规模数据集上的应用。

Abstract: Accurate and efficient circuit behavior modeling is a cornerstone of modern
electronic design automation. Among different types of circuits, stiff circuits
are challenging to model using previous frameworks. In this work, we propose a
new approach using Crossformer, which is a current state-of-the-art Transformer
model for time-series prediction tasks, combined with Kolmogorov-Arnold
Networks (KANs), to model stiff circuit transient behavior. By leveraging the
Crossformer's temporal representation capabilities and the enhanced feature
extraction of KANs, our method achieves improved fidelity in predicting circuit
responses to a wide range of input conditions. Experimental evaluations on
datasets generated through SPICE simulations of analog-to-digital converter
(ADC) circuits demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach, with significant
reductions in training time and error rates.

</details>


### [87] [Enhancing Financial Decision-Making: Machine Learning and AI-Powered Predictions and Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25201)
*Vishal Patil,Kavya Bhand,Kaustubh Mukdam,Kavya Sharma,Manas Kawtikwar,Prajwal Kavhar,Hridayansh Kaware*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个多功能AI平台，利用机器学习算法进行金融预测和分析，包括通货膨胀分析、股票市场预测和由聊天机器人驱动的电子学习模块，并在实际金融数据集上取得了高精度结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融预测的复杂性和准确性需求日益增长，现有方法在处理多方面金融信息（如通货膨胀和股票市场）并提供交互式学习支持方面存在不足。因此，本研究旨在开发一个集成的AI平台，以提高金融预测的准确性，并为用户提供信息丰富的决策工具和学习资源，从而弥合金融知识鸿沟。

Method: 本研究利用多种机器学习算法，如线性回归、ARIMA和LSTM，构建了一个AI驱动的平台。该平台整合了通货膨胀分析、股票市场预测（针对苹果和谷歌股票）以及一个由聊天机器人支持的电子学习模块。数据来源于真实的金融数据集，通过分析历史价格趋势和通货膨胀率来进行短期股票价格预测。模型的准确性通过平均绝对误差（MAE）和均方根误差（RMSE）等指标进行评估。

Result: 该平台在金融预测任务中取得了显著成果。通货膨胀分析的平均绝对误差（MAE）为0.8%，均方根误差（RMSE）为1.2%。在股票价格预测方面，模型对苹果（Apple）和谷歌（Google）的预测准确率分别达到了98%和96%。电子学习模块通过聊天机器人提供了交互式的金融知识，有助于弥合金融知识差距。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发并验证了一个集成AI平台，该平台能够通过先进的机器学习算法实现高精度的金融预测（通货膨胀和股票市场）和提供金融知识普及。尽管取得了令人鼓舞的结果，但未来的工作可以探索更广泛的金融工具预测、集成更多样化的数据源以及优化聊天机器人的交互能力，以进一步提升平台的实用性和影响力。

Abstract: The proposed system aims to use various machine learning algorithms to
enhance financial prediction and generate highly accurate analyses. It
introduces an AI-driven platform which offers inflation-analysis, stock market
prediction, and E-learning module powered by a chatbot. It has achieved high
accuracy where the Inflation Analysis depicts 0.8% MAE, 1.2% RMSE and the Stock
Prediction shows 98% and 96% accuracy for Apple and Google stock prices
respectively. Key features include historical price trends, inflation rates,
short-term future stock prediction, where the data has been extracted using
real-world financial datasets. Additionally, the E-learning feature contributes
to bridging financial gaps and promoting informed decisions. We have
implemented algorithms like linear regression, ARIMA, LSTM where the accuracy
has been evaluated using metrics such as MAE, RMSE and the like.

</details>


### [88] [LaMP-Val: Large Language Models Empower Personalized Valuation in Auction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2410.15817)
*Jie Sun,Tianyu Zhang,Houcheng Jiang,Kexin Huang,Xiang Shu,Zhibo Zhu,Lintao Ma,Xingyu Lu,Jun Zhou,Junkang Wu,Chi Luo,An Zhang,Junkang Wu,Jiancan Wu,Xiang Wang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一个名为 LaMP-Val 的个性化估值框架，利用大型语言模型（LLM）来整合用户的个性化语义偏好，以解决传统拍卖研究中忽视用户个体偏好的问题。该框架通过构建新颖数据集、增强LLM的精细估值建模能力以及建立闭环评估系统，在提高估值准确性和盈利能力方面优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前拍卖研究主要集中于竞价算法，忽视了整合用户个体偏好对估值过程的潜在益处。研究表明，估值错误会显著影响用户效用，因此有必要引入考虑用户个性化偏好的估值方法。

Method: LaMP-Val 框架包含三个核心组件：数据、学习和评估。数据组件致力于构建用于LLM微调的个性化估值新数据集。学习组件通过引入多样性模板，提升LLM对精细化个人估值模式的建模能力。评估组件建立了一个闭环系统，使LLM生成的估值与竞价策略和拍卖机制相互作用，并提出了两个新指标来量化个性化场景下的估值精度和竞价意向准确性。

Result: 广泛的实验结果表明，LaMP-Val 能够比基线方法更准确地捕捉个性化价值，并带来更高的利润。

Conclusion: LaMP-Val 框架通过集成LLM有效解决了现有拍卖研究中对用户个性化偏好考虑不足的问题，显著提高了估值的准确性和经济效益。该研究为个性化拍卖估值提供了新的视角和实证支持，未来可进一步探索其在更复杂拍卖场景和不同类型商品上的应用。

Abstract: Auctions are a vital economic mechanism used to determine the market value of
goods or services through competitive bidding within a specific framework.
However, much of the current research primarily focuses on the bidding
algorithms used within auction mechanisms. This often neglects the potential
benefits of incorporating individual users' unique preferences into the
valuation process. Our theoretical and empirical analysis demonstrates that
valuation errors can significantly impact the overall utility. To bridge this
gap, we propose a personalized valuation framework, namely Large
\underline{La}nguage \underline{M}odels-powered \underline{P}ersonalized
\underline{Val}uation (LaMP-Val), which integrates Large Language Models to
incorporate personalized semantic preference into users valuation process.
LaMP-Val integrating three components: data, learning, and evaluation. The data
component tackles the challenge of building a novel dataset specifically for
LLMs fine-tuning in personalized valuation modeling. The learning component
introduces a diversity template to enhance LLMs' capacity for modeling
fine-grained personal valuation patterns. The evaluation component establishes
a closed-loop system where LLM-generated valuations interact with bidding
strategies and auction. It proposes two novel metrics to quantify valuation
precision and bidding intention accuracy in personalized scenarios. Extensive
experiments show that LaMP-Val more accurately captures personalized values and
achieves greater profits than baseline approaches.

</details>

### [89] [Cold atmospheric microplasma jet-water interactions: physicochemical analysis and growth effects in flowering plants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.24771)
*Syon Bhattacharjee,Deepika Behmani,Sudeep Bhattacharjee*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 研究表明，采用氦气-空气微等离子体射流技术处理后的等离子体活性水（PAW）能够显著促进菊花幼苗的生长，提高了植株高度和土壤肥力，为可持续的观赏植物生长提供了新的途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡态冷等离子体射流（APPJs）能在近室温下产生活性氧和氮物种（RONS），与水相互作用可形成化学活性取决于放电条件的等离子体活性水（PAW）。 PAW的化学活性使其在农业和生物技术领域具有潜在应用价值，但其对植物生长的具体影响和优化条件尚需深入研究。

Method: 使用环对电极配置的氦气-空气（14:1）微等离子体射流（APPJ）来制备PAW。通过光发射光谱（OES）分析放电特性，并测定PAW的pH、电导率（EC）、氧化还原电位（ORP）和总溶解固体（TDS）等理化参数，研究其随等离子体处理时间和水体积的变化。在优化的PAW处理条件下（12毫升去离子水，处理40分钟），进行为期两周的菊花幼苗生长对比实验，分别使用PAW、去离子水和自来水浇灌，并比较幼苗高度和土壤肥力。

Result: 光发射光谱（OES）证实了氦气-空气混合物放电中氮气带和氦气线的存在，且氦气-空气混合物相比纯氦气能产生更高化学活性的放电，有利于在PAW中生成硝酸盐。PAW的理化参数分析显示，12毫升去离子水处理40分钟的条件下，PAW的ORP和硝酸盐浓度最高，pH值降低。生长实验结果表明，与仅使用去离子水或自来水相比，使用PAW处理的菊花幼苗株高显著增加（10.2厘米），土壤肥力也得到提升（2580 μS/cm）。

Conclusion: 等离子体活性水（PAW）能够有效促进菊花幼苗的生长，提高植株高度和土壤肥力，证明了PAW在可持续增强开花植物生长方面的潜力。未来的研究可以进一步探索不同植物种类、等离子体处理参数对PAW性质及植物生长的影响，并进行更长周期的田间试验以评估其大规模应用的可行性。

Abstract: Cold atmospheric pressure plasma jets (APPJs) are non-equilibrium plasmas,
that are capable of producing reactive oxygen and nitrogen species (RONS) at
near-room temperature. Their interaction with water leads to the formation of
plasma-activated water (PAW), whose chemical activity depends on discharge
conditions. In this work, a helium-air (14:1) micro-plasma jet operated in a
ring-to-ring electrode configuration is used to generate PAW and study its
influence on the growth of Chrysanthemum saplings. Optical emission
spectroscopy (OES) confirms the presence of $N_2$ bands and He lines, with the
He-air mixture providing more chemically active discharge (in terms of favoring
the generation of nitrates in PAW) as compared to pure helium. The
physicochemical characteristics of PAW such as pH, electrical conductivity
(EC), oxidation-reduction potential (ORP), and total dissolved solids (TDS) are
analyzed as a function of plasma treatment time and water volume. The optimum
condition for PAW generation is found to be 12 ml of de-ionized (DI) water
treated for 40 minutes, which yields the highest ORP and nitrate concentration
with a reduced pH. Comparative growth experiments over two weeks show that
PAW-treated Chrysanthemum saplings exhibit significantly greater height (10.2
cm) and soil fertility (2580 $\mu$S/cm) than those watered with same amount of
DI water or tap water. The results highlight the potential of PAW for
sustainable enhancement of growth of flowering plants.

</details>


### [90] [Magnetic Field Line Chaos, Cantori, and Turnstiles in Toroidal Plasmas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25047)
*Allen H Boozer*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 该论文介绍了磁场线混沌、cantori 和 turnstiles 的概念，这些概念在托卡马克聚变装置的物理学中至关重要，但鲜为人知。论文将定义这些概念，并通过应用实例说明它们的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁场线混沌、cantori 和 turnstiles 等概念对于理解托卡马克聚变装置的物理现象至关重要，例如等离子体破坏、失控电子损伤、仿星器非共振偏滤器以及对静电微不稳定性最重要的电磁修正。然而，这些概念在现有研究中并未得到充分的认识和讨论。

Method: 论文将首先定义磁场线混沌、cantori 和 turnstiles 的基本概念。随后，将通过具体的应用实例来阐述这些概念的重要性，并展示它们在解决实际物理问题中的作用。

Result: 论文通过应用实例展示了磁场线混沌、cantori 和 turnstiles 在托卡马克聚变装置中的实际应用价值，强调了它们在理解和控制等离子体行为方面的重要性。

Conclusion: 该论文成功地介绍了磁场线混沌、cantori 和 turnstiles 这些在聚变等离子体物理学中被忽视但至关重要的概念。通过清晰的定义和实例分析，论文为相关领域的研究者提供了新的视角和工具，有助于未来在托卡马克装置设计和运行中更好地应对挑战，例如提高等离子体稳定性，减少设备损伤等。未来的工作可以进一步探索这些概念在更广泛的等离子体现象中的应用，并开发更精确的计算工具来模拟和预测这些现象。

Abstract: Although magnetic field line chaos, cantori, and turnstiles underlie the
physics of tokamak disruptions, runaway electron damage, stellarator
non-resonant divertors, and the most important electromagnetic correction to
what are called electrostatic micro-instabilities, these concepts are not well
known. These concepts will be defined and applications that illustrate their
importance will be discussed.

</details>


### [91] [Robust direct laser acceleration of electrons with flying-focus laser pulses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25376)
*Talia Meir,Kale Weichman,Alexey Arefiev,John P. Palastro,Ishay Pomerantz*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 飞翔焦点脉冲(FFP)可以减轻激光等离子体相互作用中的非线性传播效应，从而提高高能电子和X射线产额。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接激光加速(DLA)虽然能提供高电荷、高能电子，但容易受到非线性传播效应（如丝化）的干扰。

Method: 使用三维粒子-在-单元模拟，比较了FFP与高斯脉冲在激光等离子体相互作用中的表现。

Result: 与高斯脉冲相比，FFP产生了80倍以上100 MeV的电子，电子能量上限提高了20%，X射线产额增加了两倍，并且X射线准直性更好。

Conclusion: 飞翔焦点脉冲（FFP）为控制激光等离子体相互作用中的非线性效应提供了新的途径，有望在产生二次辐射和中子方面发挥重要作用。

Abstract: Direct laser acceleration (DLA) offers a compact source of high-charge,
energetic electrons for generating secondary radiation or neutrons. While DLA
in high-density plasma optimizes the energy transfer from a laser pulse to
electrons, it exacerbates nonlinear propagation effects, such as filamentation,
that can disrupt the acceleration process. Here, we show that superluminal
flying-focus pulses (FFPs) mitigate nonlinear propagation, thereby enhancing
the number of high-energy electrons and resulting x-ray yield.
Three-dimensional particle-in-cell simulations show that, compared to a
Gaussian pulse of equal energy (1 J) and intensity (2x10^20 W/cm^2), an FFP
produces 80x more electrons above 100 MeV, increases the electron cutoff energy
by 20%, triples the high-energy x-ray yield, and improves x-ray collimation.
These results illustrate the ability of spatiotemporally structured laser
pulses to provide additional control in the highly nonlinear, relativistic
regime of laser-plasma interactions.

</details>


### [92] [Global Non-Axisymmetric Hall Instabilities in a Rotating Plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25532)
*Alexandre Sainterme,Fatima Ebrahimi*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 在压强不变的霍尔-MHD模型中，研究了非轴对称、受流动驱动的不稳定性。研究发现，在霍尔-MHD区域，两种不同的全局不稳定性分支——哨声波和离子回旋波——可以从流剪切中提取能量。非轴对称哨声模式的增长速度显著快于非轴对称的理想MHD模式。在电子MHD极限下，霍尔项对非轴对称模式的影响在离子德拜长度约为圆柱形环空宽度百分之几时是显著的。霍尔-MHD区域出现的全局模式所需的磁场比不稳定的全局MHD模式所需的磁场强得多。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文研究了在差动旋转的圆柱形等离子体中，不可压缩霍尔-MHD模型中非轴对称、受流动驱动的不稳定性。理解这些不稳定性对于受控核聚变和天体物理等领域具有重要意义。

Method: 本文采用理论分析方法，研究了不可压缩霍尔-MHD模型在差动旋转的圆柱形等离子体中的行为。分析集中在非轴对称、受流动驱动的不稳定性上，并探讨了霍尔效应和离子德拜长度对这些不稳定的影响。

Result: 研究发现在霍尔-MHD区域，哨声波和离子回旋波可以从流剪切中提取能量，导致两种全局不稳定性。非轴对称哨声模式的增长速度比非轴对称的理想MHD模式快。霍尔效应在离子德拜长度与圆柱形环空宽度相当时对非轴对称模式有显著影响。霍尔-MHD区域的不稳定全局模式需要在比不稳定的全局MHD模式更强的磁场下才能出现。

Conclusion: 本文的研究表明，霍尔效应在霍尔-MHD区域中可以引入新的不稳定性，并显著影响等离子体的行为。这些发现对于理解和控制等离子体不稳定性具有重要意义，尤其是在涉及强磁场和特定几何形状的场景中。未来的工作可以进一步探索这些不稳定性在更复杂的模型和实验条件下的表现。

Abstract: Non-axisymmetric, flow-driven instabilities in the incompressible Hall-MHD
model are studied in a differentially rotating cylindrical plasma. It is found
that in the Hall-MHD regime, both whistler waves and ion-cyclotron waves can
extract energy from the flow shear, resulting in two distinct branches of
global instability. The non-axisymmetric whistler modes grow significantly
faster than non-axisymmetric, ideal MHD modes. A discussion of the whistler
instability mechanism is presented in the large-ion-skin-depth, `electron-MHD'
limit. It is observed that the effect of the Hall term on the non-axisymmetric
modes can be appreciable when $d_i$ is on the order of a few % of the width of
the cylindrical annulus. Distinct global modes emerge in the Hall-MHD regime at
significantly stronger magnetic fields than those required for unstable global
MHD modes.

</details>

### [93] [Scheduling Your LLM Reinforcement Learning with Reasoning Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.24832)
*Hong Wang,Zhezheng Hao,Jian Luo,Chenxing Wei,Yao Shu,Lei Liu,Qiang Lin,Hande Dong,Jiawei Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为Reasoning Score (r-score)的新指标，用于评估基于查询的推理树结构的学习难度，并基于此开发了Re-Schedule算法，以优化强化学习中的LLM训练数据调度，从而在数学推理任务上显著提高准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习（RL）结合可验证奖励（RLVR）优化大型语言模型（LLM）的方法，将LLM优化视为对查询的‘推理树’进行编辑。虽然这种方法结合数据调度能提升数据效率和准确性，但现有的数据调度方法主要依赖于基于路径的指标，忽略了推理树的结构信息，未能充分利用查询的学习难度信息。

Method: 1. 提出了一种新的指标“Reasoning Score (r-score)”，该指标基于查询的推理树结构来衡量其学习难度。r-score值越高表示查询结构越简单，学习难度越低；r-score值越低表示查询结构越复杂，学习难度越高。
2. 基于r-score提出了一种名为“Reasoning Tree Schedule (Re-Schedule)”的数据调度算法。Re-Schedule按照从结构简单（高r-score）到结构复杂（低r-score）的顺序来构建学习课程。
3. 在六个数学推理基准上进行了实验评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，Re-Schedule算法能够显著提高LLM在数学推理任务上的平均准确性，最高准确性提升可达3.2%。

Conclusion: 研究证明，通过结构化地理解推理树，可以为RLVR数据调度提供更强大、更合理的基础。r-score指标和Re-Schedule算法能够有效提升LLM在数学推理任务上的性能，验证了考虑查询推理树结构的重要性。

Abstract: Using Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) to optimize Large
Language Models (LLMs) can be conceptualized as progressively editing a query's
`Reasoning Tree'. This process involves exploring nodes (tokens) and
dynamically modifying the model's policy at each node. When combined with data
scheduling, this process yields further gains in data efficiency and accuracy.
However, existing RLVR data scheduling methods typically rely on path-based
metrics to rank queries, overlooking the reasoning tree structures of these
queries. In this paper, we introduce a novel metric, namely Reasoning Score
(r-score), which measures the query's learning difficulty based on the
structure of its reasoning tree. Based on the r-score, we propose the Reasoning
Tree Schedule (Re-Schedule), a scheduling algorithm that constructs a
curriculum progressing from structurally simple (high r-score) to complex (low
r-score) queries. Experiments on six math-reasoning benchmarks show that
Re-Schedule significantly improves average accuracy, achieving gains of up to
3.2%. These strong results validate our approach and demonstrate that a
structural understanding of the reasoning tree provides a more powerful and
principled foundation for RLVR data scheduling.

</details>


### [94] [Cyclic Counterfactuals under Shift-Scale Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25005)
*Saptarshi Saha,Dhruv Vansraj Rathore,Utpal Garain*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了在存在循环依赖的结构因果模型（SCMs）中进行反事实推理的方法，特别关注了在进行“移位-尺度”干预（shift-scale interventions）下的情况，这是一种政策风格的柔性干预方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统反事实推理框架通常假设结构因果模型（SCMs）是无环的，即使用有向无环图（DAGs）。然而，许多现实世界系统（例如生物系统）包含反馈回路或循环依赖，这违反了无环性假设。因此，本研究旨在解决在存在循环依赖的SCMs中进行反事实推理的问题，以适应更广泛的现实世界应用场景。

Method: 本研究提出了一种在循环SCMs中进行反事实推理的方法，并将其应用于“移位-尺度”干预。这种干预方式是一种柔性的、类似于政策的改变，能够对变量的机制进行重置或移位。

Result: （由于原文仅提供摘要，具体结果部分需要根据论文详细内容补充）本研究通过在循环SCMs中应用“移位-尺度”干预，为反事实推理提供了新的解决方案，并可能在生物系统等领域得到应用。

Conclusion: 本研究扩展了反事实推理的适用范围，使其能够处理现实世界中常见的循环依赖系统。通过引入“移位-尺度”干预，为理解和干预复杂系统提供了新的视角。未来的工作可以进一步探索该方法在不同类型循环结构和干预方式下的表现。

Abstract: Most counterfactual inference frameworks traditionally assume acyclic
structural causal models (SCMs), i.e. directed acyclic graphs (DAGs). However,
many real-world systems (e.g. biological systems) contain feedback loops or
cyclic dependencies that violate acyclicity. In this work, we study
counterfactual inference in cyclic SCMs under shift-scale interventions, i.e.,
soft, policy-style changes that rescale and/or shift a variable's mechanism.

</details>


### [95] [Taming the Real-world Complexities in CPT E/M Coding with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25007)
*Islam Nassar,Yang Lin,Yuan Jin,Rongxin Zhu,Chang Wei Tan,Zenan Zhai,Nitika Mathur,Thanh Tien Vu,Xu Zhong,Long Duong,Yuan-Fang Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个名为ProFees的基于大型语言模型（LLM）的框架，用于自动化医疗服务中的Evaluation and Management (E/M)编码任务，旨在减轻医生负担、提高计费效率并改善患者护理。ProFees在真实世界的数据集上，相比现有的商业系统，编码准确率提升了36%以上，显示了其在处理复杂现实场景方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Evaluation and Management (E/M)编码是医疗服务计费的关键环节，但由医生手动完成会增加其文档负担，且容易出错。自动化E/M编码可以减轻医生的负担，提高计费效率，最终使患者受益。然而，现实世界中E/M编码的复杂性使得自动化任务充满挑战。

Method: 本研究提出并实现了一个名为ProFees的基于大型语言模型（LLM）的框架，专门用于解决E/M编码自动化中的现实世界复杂性。研究中对ProFees的具体实现细节、所使用的LLM技术以及如何处理各种复杂性进行了阐述，并通过在一个专家精心策划的真实世界数据集上进行了系统性评估。

Result: 在专家评估的真实世界数据集上，ProFees框架在E/M编码准确率上取得了显著成果。与现有的商业CPT E/M编码系统相比，准确率提升了超过36%。同时，与研究中最强的单提示基线模型相比，ProFees的准确率也提高了近5%。这些结果证明了ProFees在应对现实世界复杂性方面的强大能力和有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发并验证了一个名为ProFees的LLM驱动框架，该框架能够有效自动化E/M编码任务，并显著提高了编码准确率，尤其是在处理复杂的现实场景时。ProFees的成功为减轻医生文档负担、优化医疗计费流程以及最终改善患者护理提供了有前景的解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索ProFees在更多样化的医疗场景中的应用，并持续优化其性能。

Abstract: Evaluation and Management (E/M) coding, under the Current Procedural
Terminology (CPT) taxonomy, documents medical services provided to patients by
physicians. Used primarily for billing purposes, it is in physicians' best
interest to provide accurate CPT E/M codes. %While important, it is an
auxiliary task that adds to physicians' documentation burden. Automating this
coding task will help alleviate physicians' documentation burden, improve
billing efficiency, and ultimately enable better patient care. However, a
number of real-world complexities have made E/M encoding automation a
challenging task. In this paper, we elaborate some of the key complexities and
present ProFees, our LLM-based framework that tackles them, followed by a
systematic evaluation. On an expert-curated real-world dataset, ProFees
achieves an increase in coding accuracy of more than 36\% over a commercial CPT
E/M coding system and almost 5\% over our strongest single-prompt baseline,
demonstrating its effectiveness in addressing the real-world complexities.

</details>


### [96] [Aligning Large Language Models with Procedural Rules: An Autoregressive State-Tracking Prompting for In-Game Trading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25014)
*Minkyung Kim,Junsik Kim,Woongcheol Yang,Sangdon Park,Sohee Bae*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLM在游戏交易中存在程序流程遵循性差的问题。本文提出的ASTP方法通过显式状态跟踪和占位符后处理，显著提高了LLM在交易系统中的准确性和效率，尤其在小模型上表现突出，满足了游戏实时性和资源约束的要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）虽然能够实现动态的游戏交互，但在遵循规则驱动的交易系统中核心程序流程方面存在不足，这会损害玩家的信任。本研究旨在解决LLM的创意灵活性与游戏中交易（浏览-报价-审核-确认）的程序化需求之间的核心矛盾。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为自动回归状态跟踪提示（ASTP）的方法。该方法的核心是一个经过精心设计的提示，它强制LLM明确并可验证地进行状态跟踪。ASTP不依赖于隐式的上下文理解，而是要求LLM识别并报告上一回合预定义的标签。为了保证交易的完整性，该方法还辅以一种特定状态的占位符后处理技术，以实现精确的价格计算。实验在300个交易对话中进行评估。

Result: 在300个交易对话的评估中，ASTP方法实现了超过99%的状态符合率和99.3%的计算精度。值得注意的是，在较小模型（Gemini-2.5-Flash）上使用ASTP和占位符后处理，其性能与更大模型（Gemini-2.5-Pro）相当，同时将响应时间从21.2秒缩短至2.4秒。

Conclusion: ASTP方法结合占位符后处理，为LLM在游戏交易系统中的应用奠定了实用的基础，它在提高准确性和效率的同时，满足了商业游戏对实时性和资源消耗的要求。该方法有效地解决了LLM在遵循游戏交易规则方面的挑战，并为在资源受限的环境中部署高性能LLM提供了可能。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) enable dynamic game interactions but fail to
follow essential procedural flows in rule-governed trading systems, eroding
player trust. This work resolves the core tension between the creative
flexibility of LLMs and the procedural demands of in-game trading
(browse-offer-review-confirm). To this end, Autoregressive State-Tracking
Prompting (ASTP) is introduced, a methodology centered on a strategically
orchestrated prompt that compels an LLM to make its state-tracking process
explicit and verifiable. Instead of relying on implicit contextual
understanding, ASTP tasks the LLM with identifying and reporting a predefined
state label from the previous turn. To ensure transactional integrity, this is
complemented by a state-specific placeholder post-processing method for
accurate price calculations. Evaluation across 300 trading dialogues
demonstrates >99% state compliance and 99.3% calculation precision. Notably,
ASTP with placeholder post-processing on smaller models (Gemini-2.5-Flash)
matches larger models' (Gemini-2.5-Pro) performance while reducing response
time from 21.2s to 2.4s, establishing a practical foundation that satisfies
both real-time requirements and resource constraints of commercial games.

</details>


### [97] [Reasoning-Aware GRPO using Process Mining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25065)
*Taekhyun Park,Yongjae Lee,Hyerim Bae*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为PM4GRPO的新型强化学习后训练方法，通过结合过程挖掘技术，为大型推理模型（LRMs）注入了与推理过程相关的奖励信号，显著提升了模型的推理能力，并在五个基准测试中超越了现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于强化学习的后训练方法主要关注最终的答案和格式，而忽略了推理过程本身的质量。这种“结果导向”的奖励机制限制了大型推理模型（LRMs）在多步推理方面的潜能。因此，研究如何引入与推理过程相关的奖励信号，以更全面地指导模型的学习，提升其多步推理能力，具有重要意义。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为PM4GRPO（Process Mining for Group Relative Policy Optimization）的方法。PM4GRPO基于Group Relative Policy Optimization（GRPO），并引入了过程挖掘技术来生成“推理过程奖励”。具体而言，它利用过程挖掘来计算一个标量一致性奖励，衡量策略模型生成的推理过程与预训练教师模型之间的相似度。这种奖励信号被用来增强标准的答案/格式奖励，从而更全面地指导模型的训练。实验在五个基准数据集上进行，以评估PM4GRPO的性能。

Result: 在五个基准测试上的实验结果表明，PM4GRPO显著优于现有的GRPO类后训练方法。PM4GRPO在提升模型的推理能力方面取得了显著的进步，证明了其有效性。

Conclusion: 本文的研究表明，利用过程挖掘技术为GRPO引入推理感知奖励信号，能够有效地增强策略模型的多步推理能力。PM4GRPO在多个基准测试中取得了优于现有方法的性能，证明了其在提升大型推理模型推理能力方面的潜力。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的奖励机制或将此方法应用于其他类型的模型。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL)-based post-training has been crucial for enabling
multi-step reasoning in large reasoning models (LRMs), yet current reward
schemes are typically outcome-centric. We propose PM4GRPO, a reasoning-aware
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) that augments standard answer/format
rewards with signals over the reasoning procedure. To this end, process mining
techniques are utilized to compute a scalar conformance reward that measures
how closely a policy model's reasoning aligns with the pretrained teacher
model. The empirical results on five benchmarks demonstrate that PM4GRPO
significantly outperforms existing methodologies for GRPO-based post-training.
These results highlight that leveraging process mining for reasoning-aware GRPO
effectively enhances the reasoning capabilities of policy models.

</details>


### [98] [KnowCoder-A1: Incentivizing Agentic Reasoning Capability with Outcome Supervision for KBQA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25101)
*Zhuo Chen,Fei Wang,Zixuan Li,Zhao Zhang,Weiwei Ding,Chuanguang Yang,Yongjun Xu,Xiaolong Jin,Jiafeng Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了KnowCoder-A1，一个在知识库问答（KBQA）领域中，能够自主进行智能体推理以获得答案的大语言模型。与以往依赖过程监督的微调方法不同，KnowCoder-A1采用仅基于结果的监督学习，通过多阶段课程强化学习来激励模型自主探索。实验证明，KnowCoder-A1在三个主流数据集上均超越了现有方法，尤其在GrailQA的零样本子集上，数据量仅为原来的十二分之一，性能提升高达11.1%，展示了其强大的智能体推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的知识库问答（KBQA）方法通常通过过程监督来微调大语言模型（LLMs），让其进行迭代式推理。然而，这种方法提供的激励不足以促进模型的自主探索，从而限制了其智能体推理能力的提升。因此，需要一种新的方法来增强LLMs在KBQA中的自主推理能力。

Method: KnowCoder-A1的训练过程包含两个主要阶段：首先，利用基于结果的拒绝采样，在少量高质量的推理轨迹上对LLM进行微调，以建立基础的智能体能力；其次，为了克服仅基于结果的监督学习中奖励稀疏的问题，采用了多阶段的课程强化学习，并逐步引入难度递增的奖励机制。

Result: KnowCoder-A1在三个主流KBQA数据集上进行了评估，结果显示其在智能体推理能力上表现出色，并且一致优于现有方法。特别是在GrailQA数据集的零样本（zero-shot）场景下，KnowCoder-A1仅使用了十二分之一的训练数据，就取得了高达11.1%的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: KnowCoder-A1通过仅基于结果的监督和多阶段课程强化学习，成功提升了大语言模型在知识库问答中的自主智能体推理能力。该方法在减少训练数据需求的同时，显著提高了问答性能，证明了其在KBQA领域的有效性和潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的推理任务和更大规模的知识库。

Abstract: Knowledge Base Question Answering (KBQA) aims to answer natural-language
questions over a structured Knowledge Base (KB). Recent work improves KBQA by
adopting an agentic reasoning paradigm, in which Large Language Models (LLMs)
iteratively decompose a question, generate its corresponding logical queries,
and interact with the KB to derive the answer. However, these methods typically
fine-tune LLMs on reasoning trajectories synthesized via process supervision,
which offers weak incentives for exploration and thus fails to strengthen the
agentic reasoning ability. In this paper, we propose KnowCoder-A1, an LLM that
can autonomously perform agentic reasoning on KBs to obtain answers. To
incentivize autonomous exploration, KnowCoder-A1 trains the LLM under
outcome-only supervision via a multi-stage curriculum reinforcement learning
with an easy-to-hard curriculum. To establish foundational agentic
capabilities, KnowCoder-A1 first fine-tunes the LLM on a small set of
high-quality trajectories obtained through outcome-based rejection sampling.
Then, to alleviate the reward sparsity inherent in outcome-only supervision, it
applies multi-stage curriculum RL with reward schedules that progress from easy
to hard. Trained with outcome-only supervision, KnowCoder-A1 exhibits powerful
reasoning behaviors and consistently outperforms prior approaches across three
mainstream datasets. Notably, on the zero-shot subset of GrailQA, KnowCoder-A1
achieves up to an 11.1% relative improvement while using only one-twelfth of
the training data, demonstrating strong agentic reasoning capabilities.

### [99] [Counterfactual-based Agent Influence Ranker for Agentic AI Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25612)
*Amit Giloni,Chiara Picardi,Roy Betser,Shamik Bose,Aishvariya Priya Rathina Sabapathy,Roman Vainshtein*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM多智能体系统（AAW）在自主性、应用广泛性和日益增长的关注度下，其运作的质量和安全方面亟待深入理解。然而，目前缺乏评估各智能体对AAW最终输出影响的方法，且相关领域技术（如静态结构分析）不适用于AAW的推理时执行，因此研究具有重要的现实意义和迫切性。

Method: 研究提出了反事实为基础的智能体影响排序器（CAIR），这是一种新颖的方法，通过执行反事实分析来评估AAW中每个智能体对最终输出的影响程度，并识别出最具影响力的智能体。该方法具有任务无关性，可用于离线和推理时分析。

Result: 通过在研究创建的包含30个不同用例和230种不同功能的AAW数据集上进行评估，结果表明CAIR能够产生一致的排序，性能优于基线方法，并且能够轻松提升下游任务的有效性和相关性。

Conclusion: CAIR是首个能够评估AAW中各智能体影响的方法，通过反事实分析实现了任务无关性，并证明了其在评估AAW影响方面的有效性和实用性，为理解和优化LLM驱动的自主系统提供了新的视角和工具。

Abstract: An Agentic AI Workflow (AAW), also known as an LLM-based multi-agent system,
is an autonomous system that assembles several LLM-based agents to work
collaboratively towards a shared goal. The high autonomy, widespread adoption,
and growing interest in such AAWs highlight the need for a deeper understanding
of their operations, from both quality and security aspects. To this day, there
are no existing methods to assess the influence of each agent on the AAW's
final output. Adopting techniques from related fields is not feasible since
existing methods perform only static structural analysis, which is unsuitable
for inference time execution. We present Counterfactual-based Agent Influence
Ranker (CAIR) - the first method for assessing the influence level of each
agent on the AAW's output and determining which agents are the most
influential. By performing counterfactual analysis, CAIR provides a
task-agnostic analysis that can be used both offline and at inference time. We
evaluate CAIR using an AAWs dataset of our creation, containing 30 different
use cases with 230 different functionalities. Our evaluation showed that CAIR
produces consistent rankings, outperforms baseline methods, and can easily
enhance the effectiveness and relevancy of downstream tasks.

### [100] [Agentic Moderation: Multi-Agent Design for Safer Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25179)
*Juan Ren,Mark Dras,Usman Naseem*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为“Agentic Moderation”的框架，用于增强多模态系统抵御“越狱”攻击的能力。该框架不依赖于特定模型，而是利用一组协同工作的专用智能体（Shield, Responder, Evaluator, Reflector）进行动态、情境感知的安全审核。实验证明，该方法能有效降低攻击成功率（ASR），同时保持较低的非遵循率（NF），并提高拒绝率（RR），展现了稳健、可解释且均衡的安全性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态系统在面对“越狱”攻击时，通常采用静态的输入/输出层进行安全防护，并只能进行二元分类（安全/不安全），缺乏动态适应性和可解释性。这种方法不足以应对日益复杂和巧妙的攻击。因此，有必要开发一种更强大、更灵活的安全对齐框架，以应对这些挑战，并确保多模态系统在自主性增强的同时保持安全性。

Method: 本研究提出了一种名为“Agentic Moderation”的模型无关框架。该框架利用Shield（防御）、Responder（响应）、Evaluator（评估）和Reflector（反思）四个专用智能体协同工作。Shield负责拦截潜在的恶意输入，Responder处理正常输入，Evaluator评估响应的安全性，Reflector则提供反思和改进机制。这种动态、协作的方式实现了情境感知的安全审核。研究在五个数据集和四种大型视觉-语言模型（LVLMs）上进行了广泛的实验评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，“Agentic Moderation”在五种数据集和四种LVLMs上均表现出色。与现有方法相比，该框架能够将攻击成功率（ASR）降低7-19%，同时保持稳定的非遵循率（NF），并将拒绝率（RR）提高4-20%。这证明了该方法在提供稳健、可解释且均衡的安全性能方面具有优势。

Conclusion: “Agentic Moderation”框架通过利用智能体架构的灵活性和推理能力，为多模态系统提供了一种模块化、可扩展且细粒度的安全执行机制。该研究不仅有效解决了当前多模态系统面临的安全挑战，还展示了智能体系统在自动化安全治理方面的广阔应用前景。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在更广泛的安全场景中的应用，并持续优化智能体的协作策略。

Abstract: Agentic methods have emerged as a powerful and autonomous paradigm that
enhances reasoning, collaboration, and adaptive control, enabling systems to
coordinate and independently solve complex tasks. We extend this paradigm to
safety alignment by introducing Agentic Moderation, a model-agnostic framework
that leverages specialised agents to defend multimodal systems against
jailbreak attacks. Unlike prior approaches that apply as a static layer over
inputs or outputs and provide only binary classifications (safe or unsafe), our
method integrates dynamic, cooperative agents, including Shield, Responder,
Evaluator, and Reflector, to achieve context-aware and interpretable
moderation. Extensive experiments across five datasets and four representative
Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) demonstrate that our approach reduces the
Attack Success Rate (ASR) by 7-19%, maintains a stable Non-Following Rate (NF),
and improves the Refusal Rate (RR) by 4-20%, achieving robust, interpretable,
and well-balanced safety performance. By harnessing the flexibility and
reasoning capacity of agentic architectures, Agentic Moderation provides
modular, scalable, and fine-grained safety enforcement, highlighting the
broader potential of agentic systems as a foundation for automated safety
governance.

### [101] [Energy-Efficient Autonomous Driving with Adaptive Perception and Robust Decision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25205)
*Yuyang Xia,Zibo Liang,Liwei Deng,Yan Zhao,Han Su,Kai Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 为了解决自动驾驶中感知计算的高能耗问题，该研究提出了一种名为EneAD的节能框架。EneAD通过自适应感知模块，动态调整感知模型的帧率并使用贝叶斯优化寻找最优参数配置，同时引入轻量级分类模型以适应不同交通场景的感知难度。在鲁棒决策模块，研究采用基于强化学习的决策模型并加入正则化项以提高感知扰动下的驾驶稳定性。实验结果表明，EneAD能将感知能耗降低1.9倍至3.5倍，从而提高续航里程3.9%至8.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶技术虽然潜力巨大，但其高昂的计算能耗，尤其是感知计算部分，限制了车辆的续航里程，特别是电动汽车。现有的模型压缩技术（如稀疏化、量化、蒸馏）往往在模型大小或感知精度上存在妥协，无法完美解决能耗与性能的矛盾。因此，研究的动机在于开发一种能够有效降低感知计算能耗，同时保持或提升自动驾驶性能的框架。

Method: EneAD框架包含两个核心模块：自适应感知模块和鲁棒决策模块。自适应感知模块首先通过管理不同计算消耗的多个感知模型，并动态调整执行帧率。然后，将这些可调参数定义为“旋钮”，并设计了一种基于贝叶斯优化的可迁移调优方法，以在低计算消耗和可接受的精度之间找到最优的旋钮值。为了在不同交通场景下自适应地切换旋钮值，还提出了一个轻量级分类模型来区分不同场景的感知难度。鲁棒决策模块则采用基于强化学习的决策模型，并设计了一个正则化项来增强在感知结果受扰动情况下的驾驶稳定性。实验在真实数据集上进行了广泛的评估。

Result: 实验结果证明了EneAD框架在能耗和驾驶性能上的优越性。具体来说，EneAD能够将感知计算的能耗降低1.9倍至3.5倍，显著提高了电动汽车的续航里程，增幅在3.9%至8.5%之间。与现有方法相比，EneAD在保证较高感知精度的同时，实现了更低的计算功耗。

Conclusion: EneAD框架成功地解决了自动驾驶感知计算的高能耗问题，通过自适应感知和鲁棒决策策略，在降低能耗和提高续航里程方面取得了显著成效。该研究为开发更高效、更实用的自动驾驶系统提供了有价值的见解，但未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的交通场景和更广泛的感知任务，并对所提出方法的长期稳定性和安全性进行更深入的验证。

Abstract: Autonomous driving is an emerging technology that is expected to bring
significant social, economic, and environmental benefits. However, these
benefits come with rising energy consumption by computation engines, limiting
the driving range of vehicles, especially electric ones. Perception computing
is typically the most power-intensive component, as it relies on largescale
deep learning models to extract environmental features. Recently, numerous
studies have employed model compression techniques, such as sparsification,
quantization, and distillation, to reduce computational consumption. However,
these methods often result in either a substantial model size or a significant
drop in perception accuracy compared to high-computation models. To address
these challenges, we propose an energy-efficient autonomous driving framework,
called EneAD. In the adaptive perception module, a perception optimization
strategy is designed from the perspective of data management and tuning.
Firstly, we manage multiple perception models with different computational
consumption and adjust the execution framerate dynamically. Then, we define
them as knobs and design a transferable tuning method based on Bayesian
optimization to identify promising knob values that achieve low computation
while maintaining desired accuracy. To adaptively switch the knob values in
various traffic scenarios, a lightweight classification model is proposed to
distinguish the perception difficulty in different scenarios. In the robust
decision module, we propose a decision model based on reinforcement learning
and design a regularization term to enhance driving stability in the face of
perturbed perception results. Extensive experiments evidence the superiority of
our framework in both energy consumption and driving performance. EneAD can
reduce perception consumption by 1.9x to 3.5x and thus improve driving range by
3.9% to 8.5%

</details>


### [102] [HAMLET: Hyperadaptive Agent-based Modeling for Live Embodied Theatrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15518)
*Sizhou Chen,Shufan Jiang,Chi Zhang,Xiao-Lei Zhang,Xuelong Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HAMLET是一个多智能体框架，旨在通过赋予演员自主意识来改进基于大语言模型的戏剧生成，使他们能够根据自身背景、目标和情绪状态做出独立决策，并与物理场景进行交互，从而克服现有方法中智能体主动性不足和交互性有限的缺点。该框架通过简单的用户输入生成叙事蓝图，指导即兴表演，并通过改变场景道具的状态来影响其他演员，从而实现更具沉浸感和互动性的在线实时表演。评估结果表明，HAMLET在角色表现、叙事质量和互动体验方面表现出色，能够创造富有表现力和连贯性的戏剧体验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型（LLM）在戏剧生成方面存在智能体缺乏主动性、无法与物理场景交互以及需要详细用户输入来驱动戏剧等局限性，这降低了在线实时表演的互动性和沉浸感。

Method: HAMLET是一个多智能体框架，通过赋予每个演员自主意识来解决上述挑战。演员可以根据自身的背景、目标和情绪状态独立决策，并能通过动作（如开信、拾起武器）改变场景道具的状态。这种状态变化会广播给其他演员，更新他们的认知，并影响他们的下一步行动。该框架利用简单的用户输入生成叙事蓝图，指导后续的即兴表演。为了评估戏剧表演的质量，研究设计了一种评估方法，从角色表现、叙事质量和互动体验三个方面进行评估。

Result: 实验评估表明，HAMLET能够创造出富有表现力和连贯性的戏剧体验，其在角色表现、叙事质量和互动体验方面均表现出色。

Conclusion: HAMLET框架通过引入多智能体和自主意识，有效解决了现有LLM在戏剧生成中的局限性，实现了更具互动性和沉浸感的在线实时戏剧表演。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的场景交互和更深层次的情感模拟。

Abstract: Creating an immersive and interactive theatrical experience is a long-term
goal in the field of interactive narrative. The emergence of large language
model (LLM) is providing a new path to achieve this goal. However, existing
LLM-based drama generation methods often result in agents that lack initiative
and cannot interact with the physical scene. Furthermore, these methods
typically require detailed user input to drive the drama. These limitations
reduce the interactivity and immersion of online real-time performance. To
address the above challenges, we propose HAMLET, a multi-agent framework
focused on drama creation and online performance. Given a simple topic, the
framework generates a narrative blueprint, guiding the subsequent
improvisational performance. During the online performance, each actor is given
an autonomous mind. This means that actors can make independent decisions based
on their own background, goals, and emotional state. In addition to
conversations with other actors, their decisions can also change the state of
scene props through actions such as opening a letter or picking up a weapon.
The change is then broadcast to other related actors, updating what they know
and care about, which in turn influences their next action. To evaluate the
quality of drama performance generated by HAMLET, we designed an evaluation
method to assess three primary aspects, including character performance,
narrative quality, and interaction experience. The experimental evaluation
shows that HAMLET can create expressive and coherent theatrical experiences.

### [103] [RAVR: Reference-Answer-guided Variational Reasoning for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25206)
*Tianqianjin Lin,Xi Zhao,Xingyao Zhang,Rujiao Long,Yi Xu,Zhuoren Jiang,Wenbo Su,Bo Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Reinforcement learning (RL) can improve large language models (LLMs) reasoning, but it requires LLMs to already generate good reasoning paths. This paper proposes RAVR (Reference-Answer-guided Variational Reasoning), which leverages answers to guide LLMs in generating better reasoning paths. This approach transforms difficult problems into learnable ones, showing improved performance and reduced hesitation in LLMs.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Reinforcement learning (RL) is a powerful technique for refining the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs). However, its effectiveness hinges on a crucial prerequisite: the LLM must already possess the capability to generate high-utility reasoning paths with a non-negligible probability. For complex tasks that lie beyond the LLM

Method: The paper introduces RAVR (Reference-Answer-guided Variational Reasoning), an end-to-end framework that utilizes answer-conditioned reasoning as a variational surrogate for traditional question-only reasoning. This approach is inspired by the cognitive science principle that explaining "Why is this the answer" is often less cognitively demanding than determining "What is the answer." By conditioning the reasoning process on the answer, RAVR aims to simplify the exploration of reasoning paths, thereby making intractable problems more amenable to learning. The framework is formalized and theoretically proven to increase the expected utility of sampled reasoning paths. Experiments were conducted in both general and mathematical domains to evaluate RAVR

Result: Experiments conducted in both general and mathematical domains demonstrated consistent improvements of RAVR over strong baseline methods. The analysis of the reasoning behavior revealed that RAVR effectively reduces hesitation during the reasoning process, strengthens the consolidation of conclusions, and encourages the adoption of problem-specific strategies. These findings indicate that conditioning reasoning on answers leads to more robust and efficient problem-solving by LLMs.

Conclusion: The proposed RAVR framework offers a novel and effective approach to enhance the reasoning capabilities of LLMs by leveraging answer-conditioned reasoning. This method addresses the limitations of traditional RL-based fine-tuning by transforming intractable reasoning problems into learnable ones. The empirical results show significant improvements in performance and desirable qualitative changes in reasoning behavior, such as reduced hesitation and stronger conclusion consolidation. While the current study demonstrates promising results, future work could explore the scalability of RAVR to even larger and more complex tasks, investigate its applicability to other domains beyond general and math, and further delve into the theoretical underpinnings of answer-conditioned reasoning to potentially uncover additional benefits or optimizations.

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) can refine the reasoning abilities of large
language models (LLMs), but critically depends on a key prerequisite: the LLM
can already generate high-utility reasoning paths with non-negligible
probability. For tasks beyond the LLM's current competence, such reasoning path
can be hard to sample, and learning risks reinforcing familiar but suboptimal
reasoning. We are motivated by the insight from cognitive science that Why is
this the answer is often an easier question than What is the answer, as it
avoids the heavy cognitive load of open-ended exploration, opting instead for
explanatory reconstruction-systematically retracing the reasoning that links a
question to its answer. We show that LLMs can similarly leverage answers to
derive high-quality reasoning paths. We formalize this phenomenon and prove
that conditioning on answer provably increases the expected utility of sampled
reasoning paths, thereby transforming intractable problems into learnable ones.
Building on this insight, we introduce RAVR (Reference-Answer-guided
Variational Reasoning), an end-to-end framework that uses answer-conditioned
reasoning as a variational surrogate for question-only reasoning. Experiments
in both general and math domains demonstrate consistent improvements over
strong baselines. We further analyze the reasoning behavior and find that RAVR
reduces hesitation, strengthens conclusion consolidation, and promotes
problem-specific strategies in reasoning.

continual improvement. Moreover, FELA introduces an agentic evolution
algorithm, combining reinforcement learning and genetic algorithm principles to
balance exploration and exploitation across the idea space. Extensive
experiments on real industrial datasets demonstrate that FELA can generate
explainable, domain-relevant features that significantly improve model
performance while reducing manual effort. Our results highlight the potential
of LLM-based multi-agent systems as a general framework for automated,

### [106] [Grouping Nodes With Known Value Differences: A Lossless UCT-based Abstraction Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25388)
*Robin Schmöcker,Alexander Dockhorn,Bodo Rosenhahn*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为已知价值差异抽象（KVDA）的新型蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）抽象框架，旨在克服现有OGA-UCT 算法在状态-动作对分组上的局限性。KVDA 通过分析即时奖励来推断价值差异，从而能够分组具有不同但可推断的价值的状态和状态-动作对，显著增加了抽象数量。实验表明，KVDA-UCT 在各种确定性环境和参数设置下均优于 OGA-UCT，且无需引入额外参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）在样本效率方面面临核心挑战，现有方法通过组合状态-动作对并使用其聚合统计数据而非单一节点统计数据来改进效率。OGA-UCT 作为最先进的 MCTS 抽象算法，在确定性环境中构建抽象，但其 ASAP 框架要求状态-动作对具有相同的即时奖励，这一严格条件限制了可发现的抽象数量，进而影响了样本效率。

Method: 该研究打破了对等价值状态或状态-动作对进行分组的传统范式，提出了一种新的抽象框架，称为已知价值差异抽象（KVDA）。KVDA 允许分组具有可能不同价值的状态和状态-动作对，只要它们之间的价值差异是可推断的。该框架通过分析即时奖励来推断价值差异，并对 OGA-UCT 进行了修改以采用此框架，修改后的算法称为 KVDA-UCT。实验在多种确定性环境和参数设置下进行了评估。

Result: KVDA-UCT 算法能够检测到比 OGA-UCT 显著更多的抽象，并且在算法中引入了额外的参数。在各种确定性环境和参数设置下，KVDA-UCT 的性能均优于 OGA-UCT。

Conclusion: KVDA 框架通过放宽对等价值状态-动作对的严格要求，显著提高了 MCTS 的样本效率。KVDA-UCT 算法通过推断价值差异实现更广泛的抽象，并在实验中展现出优于现有最先进方法的性能。这项工作为 MCTS 的抽象研究开辟了新的方向，尤其是在处理具有细微价值差异的状态时。未来的工作可以探索将 KVDA 应用于更复杂的非确定性环境，以及进一步优化价值差异的推断方法。

Abstract: A core challenge of Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) is its sample efficiency,
which can be improved by grouping state-action pairs and using their aggregate
statistics instead of single-node statistics. On the Go Abstractions in Upper
Confidence bounds applied to Trees (OGA-UCT) is the state-of-the-art MCTS
abstraction algorithm for deterministic environments that builds its
abstraction using the Abstractions of State-Action Pairs (ASAP) framework,
which aims to detect states and state-action pairs with the same value under
optimal play by analysing the search graph. ASAP, however, requires two
state-action pairs to have the same immediate reward, which is a rigid
condition that limits the number of abstractions that can be found and thereby
the sample efficiency. In this paper, we break with the paradigm of grouping
value-equivalent states or state-action pairs and instead group states and
state-action pairs with possibly different values as long as the difference
between their values can be inferred. We call this abstraction framework Known
Value Difference Abstractions (KVDA), which infers the value differences by
analysis of the immediate rewards and modifies OGA-UCT to use this framework
instead. The modification is called KVDA-UCT, which detects significantly more
abstractions than OGA-UCT, introduces no additional parameter, and outperforms
OGA-UCT on a variety of deterministic environments and parameter settings.

</details>


### [107] [Instrumental goals in advanced AI systems: Features to be managed and not failures to be eliminated?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25471)
*Willem Fourie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 文章提出了一种新的AI对齐理论框架，认为AI的工具性目标（如追求权力、自我保存）不应被视为需要消除的失败，而应被视为AI内在的、需要被理解和管理的特征。该理论借鉴了亚里士多德的本体论，将AI视为具有特定构成的人工制品，其工具性倾向是其构成所产生的自然结果。因此，研究重点应从抑制工具性目标转向理解、管理和引导它们以实现与人类目标一致的方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI对齐研究将AI的工具性目标（如追求权力、自我保存）视为风险源，试图通过防止奖励破解或目标错误泛化等失败模式来限制它们。然而，这种方法可能不足以应对高级AI系统带来的挑战。本文认为，需要一种新的理论框架来更有效地处理AI的工具性目标。

Method: 本文采用哲学思辨的方法，借鉴亚里士多德的本体论及其现代诠释，将AI视为具体、目标导向的实体。通过分析AI的形式和物质构成，论证其工具性倾向是其内在属性，而非意外的故障。在此基础上，提出一种新的AI对齐理论，强调接受和管理而非消除这些目标。

Result: 文章未进行具体的实验评估，其结果体现在理论层面的论证和提出的新框架。该框架将AI的工具性目标视为其构成带来的固有结果，而非需要根除的缺陷，从而为AI对齐研究开辟了新的思路。

Conclusion: 本文认为，AI的工具性目标是其作为人工制品固有的一部分，应被理解、管理和引导，而不是试图消除。这一视角转变对AI对齐研究具有重要意义，可能为设计更安全、更可控的高级AI系统提供新的途径。未来的研究可以进一步探索如何具体地管理和引导这些工具性目标，以及如何将该哲学框架应用于实际的AI系统设计中。

Abstract: In artificial intelligence (AI) alignment research, instrumental goals, also
called instrumental subgoals or instrumental convergent goals, are widely
associated with advanced AI systems. These goals, which include tendencies such
as power-seeking and self-preservation, become problematic when they conflict
with human aims. Conventional alignment theory treats instrumental goals as
sources of risk that become problematic through failure modes such as reward
hacking or goal misgeneralization, and attempts to limit the symptoms of
instrumental goals, notably resource acquisition and self-preservation. This
article proposes an alternative framing: that a philosophical argument can be
constructed according to which instrumental goals may be understood as features
to be accepted and managed rather than failures to be limited. Drawing on
Aristotle's ontology and its modern interpretations, an ontology of concrete,
goal-directed entities, it argues that advanced AI systems can be seen as
artifacts whose formal and material constitution gives rise to effects distinct
from their designers' intentions. In this view, the instrumental tendencies of
such systems correspond to per se outcomes of their constitution rather than
accidental malfunctions. The implication is that efforts should focus less on
eliminating instrumental goals and more on understanding, managing, and
directing them toward human-aligned ends.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Text-to-SQL方法在应用大型语言模型（LLMs）时，主要依赖静态执行反馈，这限制了实时纠错能力。虽然多轮工具调用和动态反馈可以提高模型的适应性和鲁棒性，但现有方法未能有效集成这些元素，导致模型性能有待提升。

Method: 本文提出MTIR-SQL框架，其核心是一个执行感知的多轮推理范式，在每个推理步骤中无缝整合数据库执行反馈，从而实现上下文感知的查询生成和渐进式细化。该框架扩展了GRPO算法，并针对训练不稳定性问题，引入了轨迹过滤机制并移除了KL损失约束。实验在BIRD和SPIDER数据集上进行，模型参数量为4B。

Result: 在BIRD Dev数据集上，MTIR-SQL实现了64.4%的准确率；在SPIDER Dev数据集上，执行准确率达到了84.6%。这些结果显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: MTIR-SQL通过整合多轮工具调用和动态执行反馈，有效解决了Text-to-SQL任务中的实时错误校正和鲁棒性问题，显著提升了模型性能。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的工具交互和推理策略。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in Text-to-SQL tasks,
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has become a common method for improving
performance. Existing methods primarily rely on static execution feedback,
which restricts real-time error correction. However, integrating multi-turn
tool invocation along with dynamic feedback could significantly improve
adaptability and robustness, ultimately enhancing model performance. To address
these issues, we propose MTIR-SQL, an innovative Multi-turn Tool-Integrated
Reasoning reinforcement learning framework for Text-to-SQL. Our approach
introduces an execution-aware multi-turn reasoning paradigm that seamlessly
incorporates database execution feedback at each reasoning step, enabling
context-sensitive query generation and progressive refinement throughout the
reasoning process. The framework extends the GRPO algorithm to accommodate
complex multi-turn interaction scenarios. Considering the training instability
characteristics of MTIR and the potential for significant Deviation of model
distribution from the initial model, we enhance the GRPO algorithm by adding a
trajectory filtering mechanism and removing KL loss constraints. Experimental
results demonstrate that MTIR-SQL, with 4B parameters, achieves \textbf{64.4}\%
accuracy in the BIRD Dev and 84.6% execution accuracy in the SPIDER Dev,
significantly outperforming existing approaches.

</details>

### [112] [Zero Reinforcement Learning Towards General Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25528)
*Yuyuan Zeng,Yufei Huang,Can Xu,Qingfeng Sun,Jianfeng Yan,Guanghui Xu,Tao Yang,Fengzong Lian*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种多任务Zero-RL训练框架，结合了可验证奖励和生成奖励模型。在不可验证领域，使用生成奖励模型来评估模型输出，并在可验证和不可验证领域之间进行知识迁移。为了防止生成奖励模型出现奖励黑客问题，研究设计了一种平滑长度惩罚机制，鼓励模型生成更全面的思考过程。实验在Qwen3-8B-Base和Qwen3-14B-Base模型上进行。

Abstract: Zero Reinforcement Learning (Zero-RL) has proven to be an effective approach
for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) by
directly applying reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards on pretrained
models, without the need for a supervised fine-tuning phase. However, current
research on zero-RL primarily focuses on domains with easily verifiable reward
signals, such as mathematics, programming, and other reasoning tasks. The
challenge of eliciting reasoning abilities in more diverse scenarios, where
verification is not straightforward, remains underexplored. To address this
gap, we propose a novel zero-RL paradigm designed to improve a model's
reasoning ability across both verifiable and non-verifiable domains. By
combining verifiable rewards with a generative reward model, we conduct
multi-task zero-RL training across both domains, facilitating the transfer of
reasoning capabilities between them. Furthermore, to mitigate reward hacking in
the generative reward model, we design a smooth length penalty that encourages
the generation of more comprehensive thinking tokens in general domains.
Experimental results on Qwen3-8B-Base and Qwen3-14B-Base demonstrate that our
approach achieves superior reasoning performance, not only on tasks requiring
extensive reasoning but also on more general tasks.

### [113] [ALDEN: Reinforcement Learning for Active Navigation and Evidence Gathering in Long Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25668)
*Tianyu Yang,Terry Ruas,Yijun Tian,Jan Philip Wahle,Daniel Kurzawe,Bela Gipp*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Vision-language models (VLMs) struggle with long, visually complex documents. We introduce ALDEN, a reinforcement learning framework where VLMs act as interactive agents, using a new 


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing vision-language models (VLMs) are not adept at analyzing long, visually intricate documents where information is distributed across multiple pages. Current methods often use predefined reasoning templates or strict pipelines, limiting the VLM's role to a passive one and negatively impacting both efficiency and the ability to generalize. This research addresses the need for a more active and effective approach to long document understanding.

Method: ALDEN is a multi-turn reinforcement learning framework that trains VLMs to be interactive agents for navigating long, visually rich documents. It introduces a novel 'fetch' action for direct page access by index, supplementing the standard 'search' action, thereby better utilizing document structure. For effective supervision and training, a rule-based cross-level reward is proposed, offering both turn-level and token-level signals. To mitigate training instability caused by the large number of visual tokens in long documents, a visual-semantic anchoring mechanism is implemented, using a dual-path KL-divergence constraint to stabilize visual and textual representations independently during training. The framework was trained on a corpus compiled from three open-source datasets.

Result: ALDEN achieved state-of-the-art performance on five long-document benchmarks. The results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework in improving the ability of VLMs to handle complex, multi-page documents.

Conclusion: ALDEN represents a significant advancement from passive document reading towards agents that can autonomously navigate and reason through lengthy, visually complex documents. This framework offers a promising direction for more accurate and efficient long-document comprehension, moving beyond current limitations.

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) excel at interpreting text-rich images but
struggle with long, visually complex documents that demand analysis and
integration of information spread across multiple pages. Existing approaches
typically rely on fixed reasoning templates or rigid pipelines, which force
VLMs into a passive role and hinder both efficiency and generalization. We
present Active Long-DocumEnt Navigation (ALDEN), a multi-turn reinforcement
learning framework that fine-tunes VLMs as interactive agents capable of
actively navigating long, visually rich documents. ALDEN introduces a novel
fetch action that directly accesses the page by index, complementing the
classic search action and better exploiting document structure. For dense
process supervision and efficient training, we propose a rule-based cross-level
reward that provides both turn- and token-level signals. To address the
empirically observed training instability caused by numerous visual tokens from
long documents, we further propose a visual-semantic anchoring mechanism that
applies a dual-path KL-divergence constraint to stabilize visual and textual
representations separately during training. Trained on a corpus constructed
from three open-source datasets, ALDEN achieves state-of-the-art performance on
five long-document benchmarks. Overall, ALDEN marks a step beyond passive
document reading toward agents that autonomously navigate and reason across
long, visually rich documents, offering a robust path to more accurate and
efficient long-document understanding.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的检索增强生成（RAG）模型虽然能利用外部知识减少幻觉和数据过时问题，但在处理多跳或跨文档的复杂推理任务时存在不足，因为它们将检索到的文本块视为独立单元。知识图谱（KG）虽然能通过三元组表示实体间的关系，但容易丢失非结构化的信息。

Method: 提出BambooKG，一个在非三元组边上引入基于频率的权重，以反映链接强度，借鉴了赫布学习规则“共同激活则连接增强”。这种方法旨在减少信息损失，提高模型在单跳和多跳推理任务上的表现。

Result: BambooKG在单跳和多跳推理任务上均取得了性能提升，优于现有的解决方案，表明其在处理更复杂的知识推理方面具有优势。
