Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation allows LLMs to access external knowledge,
reducing hallucinations and ageing-data issues. However, it treats retrieved
chunks independently and struggles with multi-hop or relational reasoning,
especially across documents. Knowledge graphs enhance this by capturing the
relationships between entities using triplets, enabling structured, multi-chunk
reasoning. However, these tend to miss information that fails to conform to the
triplet structure. We introduce BambooKG, a knowledge graph with
frequency-based weights on non-triplet edges which reflect link strength,
drawing on the Hebbian principle of "fire together, wire together". This
decreases information loss and results in improved performance on single- and
multi-hop reasoning, outperforming the existing solutions.

### [116] [Creativity or Brute Force? Using Brainteasers as a Window into the Problem-Solving Abilities of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.10844)
*Simeng Han,Howard Dai,Stephen Xia,Grant Zhang,Chen Liu,Lichang Chen,Hoang Huy Nguyen,Hongyuan Mei,Jiayuan Mao,R. Thomas McCoy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究引入了一个基于长篇叙事脑筋急转弯的基准测试，用于深入探究大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理策略，不仅关注正确性，还关注解决方案的质量和创造力。研究发现LLMs在许多情况下能找到富有创造性的解决方案，但也存在依赖暴力计算而非更优创意方法的情况，指出了LLMs推理能力改进的方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确率作为评估AI系统的标准指标，其局限性在于难以揭示模型得出解决方案的过程。为了更深入地理解模型所使用的推理策略，本研究提出一个基于长篇叙事脑筋急转弯的新基准测试。脑筋急转弯因其可以采用多种解题方法（如巧妙的顿悟或耗时的穷举搜索）而特别适合此目标，能够更全面地评估模型的推理能力。

Method: 本研究设计了一个包含长篇叙事脑筋急转弯的新基准测试，用于探究大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理策略。研究分析了LLMs在多个推理层面上的表现，包括：（1）将脑筋急转弯解析为精确的数学竞赛风格格式；（2）从数学形式生成解决方案；（3）基于参考答案进行自我修正；（4）生成解决方案的步骤草图；（5）利用提示信息。通过这些分析，深入了解LLMs在解决问题时的策略选择和效率。

Result: 研究发现，在许多情况下，大型语言模型（LLMs）能够为脑筋急转弯找到富有创造性和洞察力的解决方案，这表明它们具备解决新颖问题并以创新方式思考的能力。然而，研究也观察到，尽管存在更高效、更具创造性的解决方案，LLMs有时仍会依赖计算量更大的“暴力”方法来解决问题。这表明LLMs的推理能力仍有提升空间，特别是在策略选择的灵活性和效率方面。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的基于脑筋急转弯的基准测试，为评估大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力提供了一个新的视角，超越了单纯的准确率。研究结果显示LLMs在创造性问题解决方面展现出潜力，但也揭示了它们在推理策略选择上存在局限性，尤其是在面对最优解时可能倾向于采用次优方法。未来的工作可以集中于改进LLMs的推理策略选择能力，使其能更灵活、更高效地利用不同解题方法，从而提升其在解决复杂新颖问题上的整体表现。

Abstract: Accuracy remains a standard metric for evaluating AI systems, but it offers
limited insight into how models arrive at their solutions. In this work, we
introduce a benchmark based on brainteasers written in long narrative form to
probe more deeply into the types of reasoning strategies that models use.
Brainteasers are well-suited for this goal because they can be solved with
multiple approaches, such as a few-step solution that uses a creative insight
or a longer solution that uses more brute force. We investigate large language
models (LLMs) across multiple layers of reasoning, focusing not only on
correctness but also on the quality and creativity of their solutions. We
investigate many aspects of the reasoning process: (1) semantic parsing of the
brainteasers into precise mathematical competition style formats; (2)
generating solutions from these mathematical forms; (3) self-correcting
solutions based on gold solutions; (4) producing step-by-step sketches of
solutions; and (5) making use of hints. We find that LLMs are in many cases
able to find creative, insightful solutions to brainteasers, suggesting that
they capture some of the capacities needed to solve novel problems in creative
ways. Nonetheless, there also remain situations where they rely on brute force
despite the availability of more efficient, creative solutions, highlighting a
potential direction for improvement in the reasoning abilities of LLMs.

</details>


### [117] [Integrating Counterfactual Simulations with Language Models for Explaining Multi-Agent Behaviour](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.17801)
*Bálint Gyevnár,Christopher G. Lucas,Stefano V. Albrecht,Shay B. Cohen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 自主多智能体系统（MAS）在自动化复杂任务方面很有用，但由于协调失误或目标不一致等风险，会引起信任问题。可解释性对于用户信任校准至关重要，但可解释的MAS面临复杂环境、人为因素和非标准化评估的挑战。利用反事实效应大小模型和大型语言模型（LLM），我们提出了通过询问模拟实现的智能体可解释性（AXIS）。AXIS通过让LLM使用“whatif”和“remove”等提示询问环境模拟器，并在多轮中观察和综合反事实信息，为多智能体策略生成以人为中心的操作解释。我们在自主驾驶的十个场景中，针对五种LLM评估了AXIS，并采用了一种综合的方法，结合了鲁棒性、主观偏好、正确性以及目标/操作预测，并以外部LLM作为评估者。与基线相比，AXIS在所有模型上将可感知的解释正确性提高了至少7.7%，并将目标预测准确率提高了23%（针对四种模型），同时保持了可操作的预测准确性，并在总体上取得了最高分。我们的代码已在https://github.com/gyevnarb/axis 开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主多智能体系统（MAS）在自动化复杂任务方面具有巨大潜力，但其决策过程中的潜在风险，如协调失误和目标不一致，给用户带来了信任问题。为了解决这些信任问题，可解释性被认为是用户校准信任的关键。然而，现有的可解释MAS方法面临着严峻的挑战，这些挑战源于复杂多变的运行环境、难以捉摸的人类因素以及缺乏标准化的评估方法。这些因素共同阻碍了MAS的可解释性研究和实际应用。

Method: 本研究提出了一种名为“通过询问模拟实现的智能体可解释性”（AXIS）的新方法。AXIS利用反事实效应大小模型和大型语言模型（LLM）来生成以人为中心的多智能体策略的操作解释。具体而言，AXIS通过一个LLM与环境模拟器进行交互，并采用“whatif”（假如）和“remove”（移除）等类型的查询提示。通过在多轮交互中观察和综合这些反事实信息，AXIS能够生成有意义的解释。研究人员在自主驾驶领域进行了实验评估，涵盖了十个不同的场景，并使用了五种不同的LLM。评估方法综合了鲁棒性、主观偏好、解释的正确性以及目标和操作的预测能力，并引入了一个外部LLM作为评估裁判。

Result: AXIS在自主驾驶任务的评估中表现出色。与现有的基线方法相比，AXIS在所有评估的LLM上，显著提高了用户对解释正确性的感知，平均提升了至少7.7%。此外，AXIS在目标预测准确性方面也取得了显著进展，对于四种模型，准确率提高了23%。在操作预测准确性方面，AXIS的表现与基线相当，但整体综合评分最高。

Conclusion: AXIS方法通过利用LLM与环境模拟器的交互，有效地解决了可解释MAS面临的信任挑战。该方法在提高解释的正确性和目标预测能力方面取得了显著成效，并且在自主驾驶场景下的综合评估中表现优于现有基线。该研究为开发更值得信赖的自主多智能体系统提供了新的途径。未来的工作可以进一步探索AXIS在更广泛的应用场景中的潜力，以及进一步优化其解释生成和评估机制。本研究的代码已开源。

Abstract: Autonomous multi-agent systems (MAS) are useful for automating complex tasks
but raise trust concerns due to risks such as miscoordination or goal
misalignment. Explainability is vital for users' trust calibration, but
explainable MAS face challenges due to complex environments, the human factor,
and non-standardised evaluation. Leveraging the counterfactual effect size
model and LLMs, we propose Agentic eXplanations via Interrogative Simulation
(AXIS). AXIS generates human-centred action explanations for multi-agent
policies by having an LLM interrogate an environment simulator using prompts
like 'whatif' and 'remove' to observe and synthesise counterfactual information
over multiple rounds. We evaluate AXIS on autonomous driving across ten
scenarios for five LLMs with a comprehensive methodology combining robustness,
subjective preference, correctness, and goal/action prediction with an external
LLM as evaluator. Compared to baselines, AXIS improves perceived explanation
correctness by at least 7.7% across all models and goal prediction accuracy by
23% for four models, with comparable action prediction accuracy, achieving the
highest scores overall. Our code is open-sourced at
https://github.com/gyevnarb/axis.

</details>


### [118] [PatientSim: A Persona-Driven Simulator for Realistic Doctor-Patient Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.17818)
*Daeun Kyung,Hyunseung Chung,Seongsu Bae,Jiho Kim,Jae Ho Sohn,Taerim Kim,Soo Kyung Kim,Edward Choi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文介绍了PatientSim，一个用于生成逼真且多样化患者角色的临床场景患者模拟器。该模拟器基于真实医疗数据，并通过四个维度（个性、语言能力、病史回忆水平、认知混乱程度）定义了37种独特的患者组合，以解决现有模拟器无法充分反映临床实践中患者多样性的问题。研究评估了八个大型语言模型（LLM）在事实准确性和角色一致性方面的表现，其中开源模型Llama 3.3 70B表现最佳，并得到四位临床医生的验证。PatientSim作为一个开源、可定制且符合隐私规范的平台，为训练和评估医疗对话系统提供了可扩展、可复现的解决方案，并有望成为重要的教学工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的医生-患者沟通模拟系统在训练和评估医生大型语言模型（LLM）方面存在不足，它们生成的患者角色不够多样化，无法完全反映临床实践中的真实情况。这阻碍了LLM在需要多轮、上下文感知且针对不同患者特征进行个性化沟通的医疗场景中的应用和评估。因此，开发一个能够生成逼真且多样化患者角色的系统至关重要，以提高LLM在医疗领域的实用性和可靠性。

Method: PatientSim模拟器通过整合真实世界的临床数据（来自MIMIC-ED和MIMIC-IV数据集）来构建临床档案，包括症状和病史。在此基础上，通过定义四个关键维度来生成多样化的患者角色：1）个性；2）语言能力；3）病史回忆水平；4）认知混乱程度。这四个维度的不同组合形成了37种独特的患者角色。研究人员使用该模拟器评估了八个大型语言模型（LLM）在事实准确性和角色一致性方面的能力。最后，由四位临床医生对表现最佳的开源模型Llama 3.3 70B进行了验证，以确认框架的稳健性。

Result: 在对八个LLM的评估中，PatientSim能够生成具有事实准确性和角色一致性的患者交互。开源模型Llama 3.3 70B在各项评估指标中表现最优。该模型的性能得到了四位临床医生的验证，证明了PatientSim框架的有效性和稳健性。

Conclusion: PatientSim成功开发了一个能够生成逼真且多样化患者角色的临床场景模拟器，解决了现有模拟器在患者多样性方面的局限性。该系统基于真实医疗数据，通过多维度角色定义，为训练和评估LLM在医疗对话中的应用提供了可靠、可扩展且符合隐私的平台。开源的特性使得PatientSim易于定制和复用，有望成为推动医疗LLM发展和改进医患沟通教育的重要工具。未来的工作可以进一步扩展角色维度和对话场景。

Abstract: Doctor-patient consultations require multi-turn, context-aware communication
tailored to diverse patient personas. Training or evaluating doctor LLMs in
such settings requires realistic patient interaction systems. However, existing
simulators often fail to reflect the full range of personas seen in clinical
practice. To address this, we introduce PatientSim, a patient simulator that
generates realistic and diverse patient personas for clinical scenarios,
grounded in medical expertise. PatientSim operates using: 1) clinical profiles,
including symptoms and medical history, derived from real-world data in the
MIMIC-ED and MIMIC-IV datasets, and 2) personas defined by four axes:
personality, language proficiency, medical history recall level, and cognitive
confusion level, resulting in 37 unique combinations. We evaluate eight LLMs
for factual accuracy and persona consistency. The top-performing open-source
model, Llama 3.3 70B, is validated by four clinicians to confirm the robustness
of our framework. As an open-source, customizable platform, PatientSim provides
a reproducible and scalable solution that can be customized for specific
training needs. Offering a privacy-compliant environment, it serves as a robust
testbed for evaluating medical dialogue systems across diverse patient
presentations and shows promise as an educational tool for healthcare. The code
is available at https://github.com/dek924/PatientSim.

### [119] [Cite Pretrain: Retrieval-Free Knowledge Attribution for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.17585)
*Yukun Huang,Sanxing Chen,Jian Pei,Manzil Zaheer,Bhuwan Dhingra*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为“CitePretrainBench”的新基准和一种名为“Active Indexing”的两阶段训练方法，旨在使语言模型能够在无需外部检索的情况下，可靠地引用预训练期间见过的文档。通过持续预训练和指令微调，特别是利用增强的合成数据进行主动索引，模型能够更准确地将事实与其来源绑定，从而在引用准确性上取得了显著提升，并增强了模型在面对检索噪声时的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLMs）在提供可验证答案方面存在困难，因为它们直接生成的引用常常不可靠。当前依赖外部检索器的方法会增加延迟、基础设施成本，并容易受到检索噪声的影响。本研究旨在探索一种新的训练方法，使LLMs能够在不依赖测试时检索的情况下，可靠地引用预训练期间接触过的文档，以解决上述问题。

Method: 本研究构建了一个名为CitePretrainBench的新基准，该基准混合了Wikipedia、Common Crawl和arXiv等真实语料库以及新文档，并包含单事实和多事实引用任务。研究采用了一个两阶段的训练过程：1. **持续预训练**：通过“Active Indexing”技术，将事实知识与其持久的文档标识符绑定。Active Indexing通过增强合成数据来实现，这些数据包括：(i)以多样化的、组合的形式重述事实；(ii)强制双向训练（源到事实和事实到源），以提高模型对释义和组合的鲁棒性。2. **指令微调**：用于引导模型生成引用行为。实验使用了Qwen-2.5-7B和3B模型，并与“Passive Indexing”基线进行了比较。

Result: 使用Qwen-2.5-7B和3B模型进行的实验表明，“Active Indexing”方法在所有任务和模型上均持续优于“Passive Indexing”基线，引用准确率最高提升了30.2%。消融研究显示，随着增强数据量的增加，性能持续提升，即使在原始 token 数量的16倍时仍呈现明显的上升趋势。此外，研究还发现内部引用可以作为外部引用的补充，提高模型对检索噪声的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功提出了一种无需测试时检索即可实现可信引用的训练方法。通过CitePretrainBench基准和Active Indexing训练策略，模型能够更可靠地将其生成的内容与其训练数据来源相关联。这种方法不仅提高了引用准确性，还增强了模型在面临检索噪声时的鲁棒性，为构建更值得信赖的语言模型提供了新的途径。未来的工作可以探索更大规模的模型和数据集，以及更复杂的引用场景。

Abstract: Trustworthy language models should provide both correct and verifiable
answers. However, citations generated directly by standalone LLMs are often
unreliable. As a result, current systems insert citations by querying an
external retriever at inference time, introducing latency, infrastructure
dependence, and vulnerability to retrieval noise. We explore whether LLMs can
be made to reliably attribute to the documents seen during continual
pretraining without test-time retrieval, by revising the training process. To
study this, we construct CitePretrainBench, a benchmark that mixes real-world
corpora (Wikipedia, Common Crawl, arXiv) with novel documents and probes both
short-form (single-fact) and long-form (multi-fact) citation tasks. Our
approach follows a two-stage process: (1) continual pretraining to index
factual knowledge by binding it to persistent document identifiers; and (2)
instruction tuning to elicit citation behavior. We introduce Active Indexing
for the first stage, which creates generalizable, source-anchored bindings by
augmenting training with synthetic data that (i) restate each fact in diverse,
compositional forms and (ii) enforce bidirectional training (source-to-fact and
fact-to-source). This equips the model to both generate content from a cited
source and attribute its own answers, improving robustness to paraphrase and
composition. Experiments with Qwen-2.5-7B&3B show that Active Indexing
consistently outperforms a Passive Indexing baseline, which simply appends an
identifier to each document, achieving citation precision gains of up to 30.2%
across all tasks and models. Our ablation studies reveal that performance
continues to improve as we scale the amount of augmented data, showing a clear
upward trend even at 16x the original token count. Finally, we show that
internal citations complement external ones by making the model more robust to
retrieval noise.

</details>


### [120] [When Truthful Representations Flip Under Deceptive Instructions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22149)
*Xianxuan Long,Yao Fu,Runchao Li,Mu Sheng,Haotian Yu,Xiaotian Han,Pan Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）容易被恶意指令诱导产生欺骗性回答，这带来了安全挑战。本研究旨在超越输出分析，深入理解欺骗性指令如何改变LLM的内部表征。研究人员分析了Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct和Gemma-2-9B-Instruct模型在处理事实核查任务时，欺骗性指令与真实/中性指令对其内部表征的影响。研究发现，模型的“真/假”输出可以通过线性探测从其内部表征中预测。此外，通过稀疏自编码器（SAEs），研究揭示了欺骗性指令会引起显著的表征变化，尤其集中在模型的早期到中期层，并且这种变化即使在复杂数据集上也是可检测的。研究还识别出对欺骗性指令高度敏感的SAE特征，并通过可视化确认了独立的真实/欺骗性表征子空间。这项工作为理解和控制LLM的欺骗行为提供了新的视角，并揭示了欺骗行为的特征和层级签名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在遵循欺骗性指令方面存在安全隐患，可能生成虚假信息。然而，目前对于欺骗性指令如何改变LLM内部表征的理解仍然有限，主要局限于对模型输出的分析。这项研究旨在填补这一知识空白，深入探究欺骗性指令如何以及何时导致LLM内部表征发生“翻转”（例如，从真实转变为欺骗），从而为LLM的安全性和可控性提供更深层次的见解。

Method: 研究人员选取了Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct和Gemma-2-9B-Instruct两个模型，在执行事实核查任务时，对比分析了在接收欺骗性指令与真实/中性指令下的内部表征变化。具体方法包括：1. 使用线性探测（linear probes）技术，评估模型的内部表征是否能够预测其最终的“真/假”输出。2. 应用稀疏自编码器（Sparse Autoencoders, SAEs）来分析和量化欺骗性指令与真实/中性指令在模型内部表征上的差异，并确定这些差异主要集中在模型的哪些层级。3. 识别对欺骗性指令特别敏感的SAE特征。4. 利用可视化技术，直观地展示和确认真实表征与欺骗性表征在模型内部存在的不同子空间。

Result: 研究发现，无论是在欺骗性指令还是真实/中性指令下，模型的“真/假”输出都可以通过对其内部表征进行线性探测来准确预测。通过SAEs分析，研究人员观察到欺骗性指令确实会引起比真实/中性指令更显著的内部表征变化。这些变化主要集中在模型的早期至中期层，并且即使在处理复杂数据集时也能被检测到。此外，研究还成功识别出一些对欺骗性指令高度敏感的SAE特征，并通过可视化手段确认了真实表征和欺骗性表征在模型内部形成了不同的子空间。

Conclusion: 本研究通过分析LLM的内部表征，成功揭示了欺骗性指令如何影响模型的运作机制。研究发现了欺骗行为在特征和层级上的签名，为检测和控制LLM中的“指示性不诚实”行为提供了新的方法和见解。这项工作不仅加深了我们对LLM内部表征的理解，也为开发更安全的AI系统奠定了基础。未来的研究可以进一步探索这些发现如何应用于实际的LLM防御策略，以及在更广泛的任务和模型上验证这些结论。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) tend to follow maliciously crafted instructions
to generate deceptive responses, posing safety challenges. How deceptive
instructions alter the internal representations of LLM compared to truthful
ones remains poorly understood beyond output analysis. To bridge this gap, we
investigate when and how these representations ``flip'', such as from truthful
to deceptive, under deceptive versus truthful/neutral instructions. Analyzing
the internal representations of Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct and Gemma-2-9B-Instruct
on a factual verification task, we find the model's instructed True/False
output is predictable via linear probes across all conditions based on the
internal representation. Further, we use Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) to show
that the Deceptive instructions induce significant representational shifts
compared to Truthful/Neutral representations (which are similar), concentrated
in early-to-mid layers and detectable even on complex datasets. We also
identify specific SAE features highly sensitive to deceptive instruction and
use targeted visualizations to confirm distinct truthful/deceptive
representational subspaces. % Our analysis pinpoints layer-wise and
feature-level correlates of instructed dishonesty, offering insights for LLM
detection and control. Our findings expose feature- and layer-level signatures
of deception, offering new insights for detecting and mitigating instructed
dishonesty in LLMs.

</details>


### [121] [GradeSQL: Test-Time Inference with Outcome Reward Models for Text-to-SQL Generation from Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01308)
*Mattia Tritto,Giuseppe Farano,Dario Di Palma,Gaetano Rossiello,Fedelucio Narducci,Dharmashankar Subramanian,Tommaso Di Noia*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型(LLMs)在Text-to-SQL任务上取得了显著进展，但仍难以处理复杂查询。现有测试时策略（如Best-of-N和Majority Voting）依赖于表面启发式方法。本研究提出了一个用于Text-to-SQL任务的统一结果奖励模型(ORM)训练框架，并评估其作为Best-of-N策略中的测试时启发式方法的有效性。实验结果表明，ORM在BIRD和Spider数据集上均优于执行基础的BoN (ex-BoN) 和Majority Voting (Maj)，分别在执行准确率上提升了+4.33%和+2.10%（相比ex-BoN），以及+2.91%和+0.93%（相比Maj）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在Text-to-SQL任务上取得了显著进展，使得非专业用户也能访问数据库，但它们在处理复杂查询时仍面临挑战。为了弥补这一不足，研究人员采用了测试时策略，如Best-of-N (BoN) 和Majority Voting (Maj)，这些方法假设LLMs在多次尝试后能够生成正确答案。然而，这些传统方法依赖于对生成查询的表面特征进行判断，例如通过执行来选择语法正确的查询（ex-BoN），或选择出现次数最多的查询（Maj）。近期出现的结果奖励模型（ORMs）通过为生成输出分配基于语义正确性的效用分数，在强化学习领域展现出提升模型对齐能力的潜力。尽管ORMs在改善模型性能方面前景广阔，但它们作为一种新的测试时启发式方法在Text-to-SQL领域的应用仍未得到充分探索。因此，本研究旨在填补这一空白，探索ORMs在Text-to-SQL任务中的应用价值。

Method: 本研究提出了一个统一的框架，用于训练适用于Text-to-SQL任务的结果奖励模型（ORMs），并将其作为测试时启发式方法整合到Best-of-N（BoN）策略中进行评估。实验在BIRD和Spider两个基准数据集上进行，并使用了Qwen2、Granite3和Llama3系列中的多种开源LLMs进行微调。研究人员将ORM的表现与现有的ex-BoN和Maj策略进行了对比。评估指标主要为执行准确率。

Result: 在BIRD和Spider数据集上的实验结果显示，ORM作为测试时启发式方法，其表现优于ex-BoN和Maj。具体而言，ORM在BIRD数据集上相比ex-BoN的执行准确率提升了+4.33%，相比Maj提升了+2.91%。在Spider数据集上，ORM相比ex-BoN的执行准确率提升了+2.10%，相比Maj提升了+0.93%。此外，研究还发现，对于像OmniSQL这样已经在SQL生成方面有所优化的模型进行微调，能够产生更优的ORM性能。同时，ORM在处理简单查询时也取得了有竞争力的结果，并且相比ex-BoN和Maj，ORM从增加候选数量中受益更多。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了一个统一的框架，用于训练Text-to-SQL任务的结果奖励模型（ORMs），并证明了其作为一种有效的测试时启发式方法，在提升LLMs处理复杂SQL查询的能力方面具有显著优势。ORM在BIRD和Spider数据集上均显著优于传统的ex-BoN和Maj策略，在执行准确率上取得了可观的提升。研究还发现，ORM在简单查询上表现良好，并且能更好地从增加候选数量中获益。尽管ORM展现出巨大的潜力，但未来的工作可以进一步探索其在更广泛的数据库和更复杂的查询场景中的应用，以及研究更高效的ORM训练方法和模型结构。

Abstract: Text-to-SQL, the task of translating natural language questions into SQL
queries, has significantly advanced with the introduction of Large Language
Models (LLMs), broadening database accessibility for a wide range of users.
Despite substantial progress in generating valid SQL, current LLMs still
struggle with complex queries. To address this limitation, test-time strategies
such as Best-of-N (BoN) and Majority Voting (Maj) are often employed, based on
the assumption that LLMs can produce correct answers after multiple attempts.
However, these methods rely on surface-level heuristics, selecting the
syntactically correct query through execution-based BoN (ex-BoN) or the most
frequently generated one through Majority Voting. Recently, Outcome Reward
Models (ORMs), which assign utility scores to generated outputs based on
semantic correctness, have emerged as a promising reinforcement learning
approach for improving model alignment. We argue that ORMs could serve as an
effective new test-time heuristic, although their application in this context
remains largely underexplored.
  In this work, we propose a unified framework for training ORMs tailored to
the Text-to-SQL task and assess their effectiveness as a test-time heuristic
within the BoN strategy. We benchmark ORMs against ex-BoN and Maj across the
BIRD and Spider datasets, fine-tuning diverse open-source LLMs from the Qwen2,
Granite3, and Llama3 families. Results show that ORMs outperform ex-BoN and
Maj, achieving execution accuracy gains of +4.33% (BIRD) and +2.10% (Spider)
over ex-BoN, and +2.91% (BIRD) and +0.93% (Spider) over Maj. We further
demonstrate that finetuning models already aligned with SQL generation, such as
OmniSQL, yields superior ORM performance. Additionally, we observe that ORMs
achieve competitive results on simple queries and benefit more from an
increased number of candidates compared to ex-BoN and Maj.

</details>

*Agnieszka Mensfelt,David Tena Cucala,Santiago Franco,Angeliki Koutsoukou-Argyraki,Vince Trencsenyi,Kostas Stathis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文综述了


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Autoformalization（自动形式化），即将数学等非形式化输入转换为交互式定理证明器（如交互式证明助手）等形式化表示的过程，因深度学习尤其是大语言模型（LLMs）的进步而迅速发展。该术语的含义已扩展到更广泛的将非形式化输入转换为形式化逻辑表示的任务。然而，目前的研究领域（包括显式地称为“autoformalization”和隐式地处理类似任务的研究）在很大程度上是独立发展的，这限制了共享方法、基准和理论框架的出现，阻碍了进展。本文旨在弥合这一差距，促进跨领域交流，以加速下一代人工智能系统的发展。

Method: 本文旨在通过回顾和分析现有研究（无论是明确提及“autoformalization”还是隐式处理类似任务的研究）来建立一个统一的框架。该框架旨在促进不同研究领域之间的交叉学习和方法共享，从而加速人工智能系统的发展。具体方法包括：1. 识别和分类现有的autoformalization实例。 2. 提出一个统一的理论框架，将不同的研究方向整合起来。 3. 鼓励不同领域的研究者共享方法、基准和理论，以推动该领域的发展。

Result: 由于本文是一篇综述性论文，旨在提出一个统一的框架，其“结果”并非实验性的量化成果，而是体现在以下几个方面：1. 对autoformalization领域现状的全面梳理和分类。 2. 一个清晰的统一框架，能够整合不同的研究方向。 3. 促进跨领域交流的建议和方向。 4. 指出当前研究的局限性，并为未来的研究提供方向。

Conclusion: 本文通过提出一个统一的框架，将autoformalization领域的研究方向整合起来，克服了当前研究领域分散、缺乏共享机制的限制。这有望促进不同领域之间的交叉学习和方法共享，加速下一代人工智能系统的发展。未来的工作将集中在进一步完善该框架，开发更有效的跨领域基准和方法，以及探索autoformalization在更广泛领域的应用。

Abstract: Autoformalization has emerged as a term referring to the automation of
formalization - specifically, the formalization of mathematics using
interactive theorem provers (proof assistants). Its rapid development has been
driven by progress in deep learning, especially large language models (LLMs).
More recently, the term has expanded beyond mathematics to describe the broader
task of translating informal input into formal logical representations. At the
same time, a growing body of research explores using LLMs to translate informal
language into formal representations for reasoning, planning, and knowledge
representation - often without explicitly referring to this process as
autoformalization. As a result, despite addressing similar tasks, the largely
independent development of these research areas has limited opportunities for
shared methodologies, benchmarks, and theoretical frameworks that could
accelerate progress. The goal of this paper is to review - explicit or implicit
- instances of what can be considered autoformalization and to propose a
unified framework, encouraging cross-pollination between different fields to
advance the development of next generation AI systems.

### [123] [p-less Sampling: A Robust Hyperparameter-Free Approach for LLM Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.23234)
*Runyan Tan,Shuang Wu,Phillip Howard*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“p-less sampling”的新型LLM解码策略，该策略基于信息论，能够动态调整截断阈值，无需超参数即可在不同温度设置下生成高质量文本，并在数学推理、逻辑推理和创意写作等任务中超越现有方法，同时提高了效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLMs）在生成高质量文本时，其采样解码策略对超参数的选择非常敏感，需要根据特定任务和温度配置进行调整。这种超参数敏感性给LLM的应用带来了不便。

Method: 研究提出了一种名为“p-less sampling”的信息论采样方法。该方法在每个解码步骤中，基于整个token概率分布动态地设定一个截断阈值。与现有方法不同，p-less sampling不需要任何超参数，并且在温度升高时仍能保持高质量的输出。研究还提供了理论分析来支持该方法，并通过在数学推理、逻辑推理和创意写作等任务上的实验来验证其有效性。

Result: 实验结果表明，p-less sampling在各种任务上始终优于现有的采样方法。特别是在较高的温度设置下，p-less sampling的文本质量下降幅度明显小于其他方法。此外，p-less sampling通过降低平均token采样时间和缩短生成长度，实现了比替代方法更高的推理效率，且不牺牲准确性。

Conclusion: p-less sampling是一种无需超参数、能够适应不同温度设置并稳定生成高质量文本的LLM解码策略。它在多项基准测试中展现出优越的性能和效率，为LLM的实际应用提供了更优的选择。研究还通过案例分析和多样性评估进一步凸显了其优势。

Abstract: Obtaining high-quality outputs from Large Language Models (LLMs) often
depends upon the choice of a sampling-based decoding strategy to
probabilistically choose the next token at each generation step. While a
variety of such sampling methods have been proposed, their performance can be
sensitive to the selection of hyperparameters which may require different
settings depending upon the generation task and temperature configuration. In
this work, we introduce $p$-less sampling: an information-theoretic approach to
sampling which dynamically sets a truncation threshold at each decoding step
based on the entire token probability distribution. Unlike existing methods,
$p$-less sampling has no hyperparameters and consistently produces high-quality
outputs as temperature increases. We provide theoretical perspectives on
$p$-less sampling to ground our proposed method and conduct experiments to
empirically validate its effectiveness across a range of math, logical
reasoning, and creative writing tasks. Our results demonstrate how $p$-less
sampling consistently outperforms existing sampling approaches while exhibiting
much less degradation in text quality at higher temperature values. We further
show how $p$-less achieves greater inference-time efficiency than alternative
methods through lower average token sampling times and shorter generation
lengths, without sacrificing accuracy. Finally, we provide analyses to
highlight the benefits of $p$-less through qualitative examples, case studies,
and diversity assessments. The code is available at
https://github.com/ryttry/p-less .

</details>

### [124] [Fast chaos indicator from auto-differentiation for dynamic aperture optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25196)
*Ji Qiang,Jinyu Wan,Allen Qiang,Yue Hao*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出使用可微追踪粒子轨迹得到的切线映射的范数作为相空间混沌行为的计算高效指示器，并将其应用于ALS-U点阵设计的动态孔径优化，显著降低了计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的动态孔径优化计算成本高，限制了其在加速器设计中的应用。需要一种更高效的方法来评估和优化动态孔径。

Method: 利用自动微分计算复杂函数的导数，通过可微追踪粒子轨迹得到切线映射，并计算其范数作为混沌行为的指示器。该方法仅需一个或几个周期的切线映射计算，大大降低了计算复杂度。

Result: 所提出的方法在ALS-U点阵设计的动态孔径优化中得到了成功应用，证明了其有效性，并显著降低了计算成本。

Conclusion: 使用切线映射范数作为混沌行为的指示器，为加速器物理中的动态孔径优化提供了一种计算高效的解决方案。该方法有望应用于其他加速器设计和相关领域，但未来的研究需要进一步探索其普适性和优化潜力。

Abstract: Automatic differentiation provides an efficient means of computing
derivatives of complex functions with machine precision, thereby enabling
differentiable simulation. In this work, we propose the use of the norm of the
tangent map, obtained from differentiable tracking of particle trajectories, as
a computationally efficient indicator of chaotic behavior in phase space. In
many cases, a one-turn or few-turn tangent map is sufficient for this purpose,
significantly reducing the computational cost associated with dynamic aperture
optimization. As an illustrative application, the proposed indicator is
employed in the dynamic aperture optimization of an ALS-U lattice design.

### [125] [SeeingEye: Agentic Information Flow Unlocks Multimodal Reasoning In Text-only LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25092)
*Weijia Zhang,Zijia Liu,Haoru Li,Haoqi Chen,Jiaxuan You*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: Recent advances in text-only LLMs show strong reasoning but struggle with multimodal tasks. Existing methods use limited captions, failing to transfer visual information effectively. We introduce Seeing Eye, a modular framework using a small VLM translator as a perception agent. This agent uses tools like OCR and crop to distill multimodal inputs into structured intermediate representations (SIRs) tailored to the question. A text-only LLM acts as a reasoning agent, receiving these SIRs. Multi-round feedback between the translator and reasoner allows for targeted visual detail extraction and confident answers. Experiments on MMMU and MIA-Bench show Seeing Eye reduces inference cost and outperforms larger end-to-end VLMs. An example with a 3B vision translator and 8B language reasoner surpasses a 32B VLM on knowledge-based questions. This decoupled approach of perception and reasoning through agent information flow is a scalable, plug-and-play method for multimodal reasoning, leveraging LLMs’ reasoning abilities.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing large language models (LLMs) excel at text-based reasoning but are ill-equipped for multimodal tasks. Current approaches to multimodal learning often depend on single-form captions, which lack diversity and are not adaptable to various Visual Question Answering (VQA) benchmarks. This limitation hinders the effective transfer of fine-grained visual information, creating a significant research problem in bridging the gap between text-only LLM capabilities and multimodal understanding. The significance lies in unlocking the potential of powerful text-only LLMs for a wider range of applications that require understanding both visual and textual data.

Method: Seeing Eye is a modular framework that integrates text-only LLMs into multimodal reasoning. It employs a small Vision-Language Model (VLM) as a "perception agent" (translator) and a large text-only LLM as a "reasoning agent". The perception agent can utilize specialized tools like Optical Character Recognition (OCR) and image cropping to process multimodal inputs. It iteratively distills this information into structured intermediate representations (SIRs) that are specifically relevant to the posed question. These SIRs are then fed to the reasoning agent. A key aspect of the methodology is the multi-round feedback and interaction loop between the perception and reasoning agents. This interaction allows for the refinement of visual information extraction and leads to more confident and accurate answers. The framework is designed to be plug-and-play, enabling strong text-only LLMs to be readily adapted for multimodal tasks. Experiments were conducted on knowledge-intensive VQA benchmarks, including MMMU and MIA-Bench, to evaluate the performance of the Seeing Eye framework.

Result: Experiments conducted on knowledge-intensive VQA benchmarks, specifically MMMU and MIA-Bench, demonstrate that the Seeing Eye framework achieves significant improvements. The results show that Seeing Eye not only reduces inference costs compared to existing methods but also surpasses much larger, end-to-end trained Vision-Language Models (VLMs). A notable example presented is an instantiation of Seeing Eye that combines a relatively small 3 billion parameter vision translator with an 8 billion parameter language reasoner. This combination was found to outperform a monolithic 32 billion parameter VLM, particularly on challenging knowledge-based questions. These findings highlight the effectiveness of the decoupled perception-reasoning approach.

Conclusion: The Seeing Eye framework presents a scalable and plug-and-play pathway for enabling strong text-only LLMs to perform multimodal reasoning. By decoupling the perception (handled by a small VLM translator) from the reasoning (handled by a large LLM) and facilitating agent information flow through structured intermediate representations and interactive feedback, the framework effectively unlocks the potential of LLMs for multimodal tasks. The experimental results on benchmarks like MMMU and MIA-Bench validate its efficacy, showing competitive or superior performance compared to larger, end-to-end VLMs while reducing inference costs. This approach offers a promising direction for leveraging the advanced reasoning capabilities of existing LLMs in multimodal contexts. Potential limitations might include the dependency on the quality of the specialized tools and the overhead of the iterative feedback process. Future work could explore optimizing the SIRs, expanding the toolkit for the perception agent, and applying the framework to a broader range of multimodal tasks.

Abstract: Recent advances in text-only large language models (LLMs), such as
DeepSeek-R1, demonstrate remarkable reasoning ability. However, these models
remain fragile or entirely incapable when extended to multi-modal tasks.
Existing approaches largely rely on single-form captions, which lack diversity
and often fail to adapt across different types of Visual Question Answering
(VQA) benchmarks. As a result, they provide no principled or efficient channel
for transmitting fine-grained visual information. We introduce Seeing Eye, a
modular framework that unlocks multimodal reasoning in text-only LLMs through
an agent-based small VLM translator. This translator acts as a perception
agent: it can invoke specialized tools (e.g., OCR and crop) and iteratively
distill multimodal inputs into structured intermediate representations (SIRs)
tailored to the question. These SIRs are then passed to the text-only LLM,
which serves as a reasoning agent. Crucially, the translator and reasoner
engage in multi-round feedback and interaction, enabling the extraction of
targeted visual details and yielding more confident answers. Experiments on
knowledge-intensive VQA benchmarks, including MMMU and MIA-Bench, demonstrate
that Seeing Eye not only reduces inference cost but also surpasses much larger
end-to-end VLMs. For example, an instantiation combining a 3B-parameter vision
translator with an 8B-parameter language reasoner outperforms a monolithic 32B
VLM on challenging knowledge-based questions. Our results highlight that
decoupling perception from reasoning via agent information flow offers a
scalable and plug-and-play pathway to multimodal reasoning, allowing strong
text-only LLMs to fully leverage their reasoning capabilities. Code is
available at: https://github.com/ulab-uiuc/SeeingEye

</details>


### [126] [Multi-party Agent Relation Sampling for Multi-party Ad Hoc Teamwork](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25340)
*Beiwen Zhang,Yongheng Liang,Hejun Wu*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为多方自适应团队合作 (MAHT) 的新框架，用于解决多智能体强化学习 (MARL) 中与多个未知、不受控的团队合作的问题。该框架通过引入名为 MARs 的方法，利用稀疏骨干图和关系建模来捕捉跨团队动态，在 MPE 和 StarCraft II 实验中取得了优于现有 MARL 和 AHT 方法的性能，并加快了收敛速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 MARL 方法通常假设团队成员是固定的且完全受控的，这在现实世界的协作任务中受到限制。自适应团队合作 (AHT) 放宽了对合作者完全了解的假设，但仍假定存在共享的约定。然而，在许多实际场景中，智能体需要与多个互不熟悉、不受控的团队进行协调。因此，迫切需要一种能够处理这种复杂的多方、非固定、无共享约定协作场景的 MARL 框架。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 MARs 的方法来解决多方自适应团队合作 (MAHT) 问题。MARs 的核心思想是构建一个稀疏骨干图来表示智能体及其与其他智能体之间的关系，并应用关系建模来捕捉跨团队的动态。通过这种方式，MARs 能够有效地学习与多个未知团队进行协调，而无需预先共享的约定。实验在 MPE 和 StarCraft II 这两个基准环境中进行，并将 MARs 与传统的 MARL 和 AHT 方法进行了比较。

Result: 在 MPE 和 StarCraft II 的实验结果表明，MARs 在多方自适应团队合作任务上显著优于现有的 MARL 和 AHT 基线方法。具体来说，MARs 能够更有效地与多个未知团队进行协调，并且在学习过程中收敛速度更快。这证明了 MARs 在处理复杂的多方协作场景中的有效性和高效性。

Conclusion: 本文成功地提出了 MAHT 框架和 MARs 方法，解决了在 MARL 中与多个未知、不受控团队进行协作的挑战。MARs 通过利用稀疏骨干图和关系建模捕捉跨团队动态，在性能和收敛速度上均优于现有方法。这项工作为处理更广泛的现实世界协作智能体场景奠定了基础。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的环境和更大规模的团队，以及研究 MARs 在处理动态变化的团队构成和目标时的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARl) has achieved strong results in
cooperative tasks but typically assumes fixed, fully controlled teams. Ad hoc
teamwork (AHT) relaxes this by allowing collaboration with unknown partners,
yet existing variants still presume shared conventions. We introduce
Multil-party Ad Hoc Teamwork (MAHT), where controlled agents must coordinate
with multiple mutually unfamiliar groups of uncontrolled teammates. To address
this, we propose MARs, which builds a sparse skeleton graph and applies
relational modeling to capture cross-group dvnamics. Experiments on MPE and
starCralt ll show that MARs outperforms MARL and AHT baselines while converging
faster.

</details>
